 

ɔd͡ʒɔ୍  at 
dɔ୍wara b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍gita rɔ pɔ୍rɔୋd͡ʒek୍ʈɔ guʈenɔbɔrɔ୍gɔ 

ibuk୍ apɔɳɔ ehaku nɔkɔlɔ kɔriparibe ehaku deiparibe kim୍ba 
ehi ibuk୍ kim୍ba ɔnɔ୍lain୍re  re 
ɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ୍b̤uk୍tɔ pɔ୍rɔୋd͡ʒek୍ʈɔ guʈenɔbɔrɔ୍gɔ laisen୍sɔ sɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tabɭi ɔnud͡ʒaji ehaku pun  bɔ୍jɔbɔhar kɔriparibe 
akʰ୍ja b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍gita 
lekʰɔkɔ benami 
ɔnubadɔkɔ sar୍ eɖwin୍ ar୍nɔୋlɔ୍ɖɔ 
pɔୋsɔ୍ʈiŋ tarikʰ 
 d͡ʒun୍ 
 
 
 
 
d͡ʒesi bair୍sɔ dɔ୍wara ut୍padit | ɔlɔ henɔsɔ୍ dɔ୍wara  sɔnsɔ୍kɔrɔɳɔ |























git sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij |
kim୍ba
b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍gita
mɔhab̤arɔtɔru
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun
b̤arɔtɔrɔ rad͡ʒkumar ebɔŋ
kr̩s୍ɳɔŋɔ୍kɔ ɔd̤inre sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ sr̩s୍ʈikɔrɔ୍tɔ୍taŋ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre ek alୋt͡ʃɔna heba |


sar୍ eɖwin୍ ar୍nɔୋlɔ୍ɖɔ

nɔ୍jujɔrɔ୍kɔ
ʈɔ୍rus୍lɔୋb̤ɔ hanɔsɔnɔ୍ aɳ୍ɖɔ kɔmɔ୍ba limiʈeɖ୍
 pɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔmɔ ab̤en୍ju

sɔmɔrɔ୍pɔɳɔ |

iɳ୍ɖiaku

teɳu mũ ehi t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar ebɔŋ at୍ma ​​rɔୋmaɲ୍t͡ʃɔkɔrɔ b̤asɔɳɔ pɔ  it͡ʃʰi
kr̩s୍ɳɔ ebɔŋ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍kɔ dɔ୍  ara pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jekɔŋɔ୍ku pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jekɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit alୋt͡ʃɔna kɔritʰile
teɳu mũ eʈʰare ehar d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan lekʰit͡ʃʰi  ehar luk୍kajit rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔ
inlɔɳɔ୍ɖɔ paĩ he b̤arɔtɔ se d͡ʒepri mɔୋ paĩ pɔ୍rij

  |





pur୍babɔlɔୋkɔnɔ
ehi pɔ୍rɔsid୍d̤ɔ tɔtʰa t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar sɔnsɔ୍kr̩t kɔbita mɔhab̤arɔtɔrɔ ek episୋɖɔ୍ b̤abre g̤ɔʈitʰae sɔsɔ୍ʈʰɔ  kim୍ba b̤is୍mɔ  mɔhan hin୍du mɔhakasɔrɔ pɔrɔb̤a | eha b̤arɔtɔre ɔpar lɔୋkɔpɔ୍rijta ebɔŋ ɔd̤ikarku upɔb̤ɔୋgɔ kɔre d͡ʒeũʈʰare ehaku debnagiri sahit୍jɔrɔ paɲ୍t͡ʃɔ d͡ʒuel୍  pɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃaraʈani b̤abre gɔɳad͡ʒae | sad̤a kin୍tu ut୍tɔmɔ b̤asare eha ek dar୍sɔnik pɔ୍rɔɳaɭiku un୍muk୍tɔ kɔre d͡ʒaha ad͡ʒi pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ bid୍jɔman bɔ୍rah୍mɔɳij ɔʈe | bis୍  as kɔpila pɔtɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔɭi ebɔŋ bedɔŋɔ୍kɔ tɔtɔ୍tɔ୍  b̤ɔɭi mis୍rit | ehar ɔnek g̤ɔୋsɔɳa ete ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ ɔʈe teɳu ehar akaŋkʰjaku ete mɔhan୍ sud୍d̤ɔ ebɔŋ d̤ar୍miktaku kɔୋmɔɭɔ kɔre d͡ʒe sɔ୍legel kɔbita ɔd̤ɔ୍jɔjɔnɔ kɔriba pɔre pɔ୍rɔbes kɔle | ehar ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲat lekʰɔkɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔ୍rɔti ehi anɔnɔ୍dɔ ebɔŋ pɔ୍rɔsɔnsa         ।      nɔ୍juminis୍kɔ haipୋpʰeʈa                                   ​​ | ehi t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar sɔ୍rɔdɔ୍d̤aɲ୍d͡ʒɔɭi lekʰɔkɔ kʰɔ୍ris୍ʈian ut୍sɔru  ɳɔ neitʰile ki taŋ୍kɔʈʰaru ib̤an୍selis୍ʈɔ ebɔŋ pɔ୍reritmane |

eha ehar tarikʰɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔsɔ୍nɔ uʈʰae d͡ʒaha sɔkɔrat୍mɔkɔ b̤abre sɔmad̤an hɔୋiparib nahĩ | muɭ mɔhab̤arɔtɔ ɔpekʰja eha ek pɔ୍rat͡ʃin mɔhakasre ɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ୍b̤uk୍tɔ hɔୋitʰla kin୍tu kʰɔ୍ris୍ʈian d͡ʒugɔrɔ pur୍bɔ pɔ୍rɔmaɳ kɔribaku sɔ୍ri kasinatʰ teleŋ୍gɔ kit͡ʃʰi d͡ʒɔtʰar୍tʰɔ d͡ʒuk୍ti upɔsɔ୍tʰapɔnɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti। pɔ୍rɔmaɳɔrɔ od͡ʒɔnɔ kʰɔ୍ris୍ʈɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔre pɔ୍raj tr̩tij sɔtab୍dire ehar rɔt͡ʃɔna sɔ୍tʰanit kɔre ebɔŋ bɔୋd̤ɔhue galilir sikʰja ebɔŋ siria ɔbɔtarɔrɔ ehi bɔ୍rah୍mɔɳɔ kɔbitare pɔ୍rɔtid୍̤wɔni ɔt͡ʃʰi |

ehar dr̩s୍jɔ heut͡ʃʰi d͡ʒum୍na ebɔŋ sɔrɔsuti nɔdibɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman kur୍nul ebɔŋ d͡ʒeɳ୍ɖɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre ek sɔ୍tɔrij des | ehar sɔrɔɭɔ sɔɖɔd͡ʒɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔre rad͡ʒa d͡ʒud̤is୍ʈʰirɔŋɔ୍kɔ b̤ai pɔ୍rin୍sɔ ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun rɔtʰɔd͡ʒat୍riŋ୍kɔ t͡ʃʰɔdɔ୍mɔbesre sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ debta kr̩s୍ɳɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhɔ ajୋd͡ʒit ek sɔɳɭap rɔhit͡ʃʰi। kɔ  rɔbɔ ebɔŋ paɳ୍ɖɔbɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔ  nɔ୍jɔbahini mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre ek bɔɖɔ଼ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ asut͡ʃʰi ebɔŋ ehi bar୍tɔ୍taɭap bipɔkʰjɔ hɔୋsɔ୍ʈɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre ɔŋɔ୍kit d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ rɔtʰɔre bɔd͡ʒaj rɔhit͡ʃʰi |

kɔbitaʈi bɔrɔ୍nɔpʰɔ୍ dɔ୍  ara pʰɔrasi b̤asare lasen୍ dɔ୍  ara laʈin୍ b̤asare sɔ୍ʈanis୍lab୍̤ gaʈiŋ୍kɔ dɔ୍  ara iʈalij b̤asare galanୋsɔ୍ dɔ୍  ara gɔ୍rik୍ b̤asare ebɔŋ inrad͡ʒire sɔ୍ri tʰɔmɔ୍sɔnɔ୍ ebɔŋ sɔ୍ri ɖab̤id͡ʒ୍ŋɔ୍kɔ dɔ୍  ara pɔriɳɔtɔ hɔୋit͡ʃʰi ses namɔrɔ gɔdɔ୍jɔ lipi pɔ୍rɔkr̩tre pɔ୍rɔsɔnsa d͡ʒɔୋgɔ୍jɔ nuhẽ। ehar bis୍wɔsɔ୍tɔta ebɔŋ sɔ୍wɔt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃʰɔta | sɔ୍ri teleŋ୍gɔ bɔmɔ୍bere bɔhub̤asi gitre ek sɔnsɔ୍kɔrɔɳɔ pɔ୍rɔkas kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒaha sikʰjit ebɔŋ bud୍d̤iman kin୍tu muɭɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍man kim୍ba ɔnug୍rɔhɔku d͡ʒɔɳai nahĩ | d͡ʒɔdi mũ bɔhu un୍nɔtɔ pɔɳɔ୍ɖitɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔre t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar kɔbitar ɔnubad pɔ୍rɔdan kɔribaku ud୍jɔmɔ kɔre tebe eha semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔris୍rɔmɔru pɔ୍rap୍tɔ sahad͡ʒ୍jɔrɔ kr̩tɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲɔtar sɔ୍wikr̩ti ɔʈe ebɔŋ lɔୋkɔpɔ୍rij sahit୍jɔre kɔbita ebɔŋ dar୍sɔnik kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ bina inrad͡ʒi sahit୍jɔ nis୍t͡ʃit b̤abre ɔsɔmɔ୍pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ heb | b̤arɔtɔku

git selɔsɔ୍ʈial୍ nid͡ʒ paĩ bɔ୍jakʰ୍ja kɔre nahĩ bɔୋli au kit͡ʃʰi kɔhibar nahĩ | sɔnsɔ୍kr̩t muɭ ɔnus୍ka miʈɔrɔre lekʰad͡ʒait͡ʃʰi d͡ʒaha pas୍t͡ʃat୍jɔ kan paĩ sɔpʰɔɭɔtar sɔhit pun  pɔ୍rɔkasit hɔୋiparib nahĩ | teɳu mũ ehaku amɔrɔ nɔmɔnij sun୍jɔ pɔdɔre pɔkai deit͡ʃʰi gitar mapre pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔ hɔୋit͡ʃʰi d͡ʒeũʈʰare paʈʰ nid͡ʒe sɔman b̤abre b̤aŋ୍ge | ɔd̤ikansɔ ɔnsɔ paĩ mũ bis୍  as kɔre nim୍nɔ pr̩s୍ʈʰare bis୍wɔsɔ୍tɔ b̤abre sɔnrɔkʰjit hebar ɔrɔ୍tʰɔ kin୍tu sɔ୍legel nid͡ʒe kɔhibaku pɔɖila rekɔɳɔ୍ɖiʈiɔribɔsɔre mɔୋte sem୍pɔrɔ୍ pɔୋʈapʰୋsɔ୍ʈɔrɔ meɳ୍ʈem rek୍ʈɔ ɖib̤inase apʰ୍rimare nɔnɔ୍ ajusim୍ | d͡ʒeũmane kɔbitar dɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ upre ɔd̤ik pɔ  ibe semane mesɔrɔ୍sɔ ʈɔ୍rɔbɔnɔrɔ୍ aɳ୍ɖɔ kɔୋ dɔ୍wara mud୍rit sɔ୍ri ɖeb̤id͡ʒ୍ŋɔ୍kɔ b̤ɔlɔ୍jumre ek pɔ୍rɔsɔnsɔnij pɔrit͡ʃɔjɔ paiparɔnɔ୍ti |

  





bisɔjɔbɔsɔ୍tu

 ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍kɔ bib̤ad͡ʒɔnɔ
 ɖɔkɔ୍ʈɔ୍rin୍ buk୍
 kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre b̤ɔrɔ୍t͡ʃɔ୍ju
। d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ  pun  nir୍maɳ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ । selɔpʰɔ୍res୍ʈɔ୍ren୍ dɔ୍  ara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ bib̤ad͡ʒɔnɔ dɔ୍  ara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ  sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ  rɔ seba dɔ୍wara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ | kɔɭiŋ୍gɔ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan ebɔŋ kɔɭiŋ୍gɔ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔ  d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ dɔ୍  ara । gɔୋʈie ebɔŋ mɔnipʰୋlɔ୍ɖɔ  rɔ pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ | bis୍wasɔrɔ d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ  bisɔjɔ ebɔŋ at୍ma ​​ rɔ pr̩tʰɔkɔta dɔ୍wara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ |










guɳɔbɔtɔ୍ta  ru pr̩tʰɔkɔta dɔ୍wara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ | sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ  pɔ୍rap୍tɔ kɔri d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ | ɖib̤ain୍ ebɔŋ junib̤ain୍  rɔ pr̩tʰɔkɔta | tɔ୍rɔjɔୋdɔsɔ bis୍was dɔ୍wara ɔsɔ୍ʈadɔsɔ | bitɔrɔɳɔ ebɔŋ pun  nir୍maɳ dɔ୍wara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ |







ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj 
d̤r̩tira
pɔbit୍rɔ sɔmɔtɔɭɔ b̤umire d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ paĩ ehipri b̤abre
 kurukʰjet୍rɔre  kuh sɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔjɔ kuh
mɔୋrɔ lɔୋkɔ o paɳ୍ɖɔbɔmane kɔɳɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
sɔ  ୍d͡ʒɔjɔ
d͡ʒetebeɭe se paɳ୍ɖɔbɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ hɔୋsɔ୍ʈɔ dekʰile
rad͡ʒa dur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔୋd̤ɔnɔŋɔ୍ku ɖɔ୍rɔୋna aŋ୍kile
ebɔŋ ehi sɔbɔ୍dɔguɖ଼ik kɔhile a  guru ehi d̤aɖ଼iʈi dekʰ
eha paɳ୍ɖu d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔpurusmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ kete bis୍tr̩t  tumɔrɔ pɔɳɔ୍ɖit
dɔ୍rɔ  pɔɖaŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ
d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ etʰire
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔri mukʰiamane rɔhit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒepri b̤ima mukʰia
d̤ɔnu bɔɳɔ୍ɖɔrɔ୍ biraʈa jujud̤an୍ dɔ୍rɔ  pɔɖa
taŋ୍kɔ karre bisis୍ʈɔ dɔ୍rɔ  pɔdɔkɔ t͡ʃekiʈan୍ kasiŋ୍kɔ
sɔ୍ʈauʈ୍ pɔ୍rɔb̤u
purd͡ʒit୍ kuɳ୍ʈib̤ୋd͡ʒɔ ebɔŋ saib̤ja
d͡ʒudamanuju sɔhit
sub̤ɔdɔ୍raŋ୍kɔ pila ebɔŋ dɔ୍rɔ  pɔdiŋ୍kɔ  sɔmɔsɔ୍te pɔ୍rɔsid୍d̤ɔ
sɔmɔsɔ୍te semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ rɔtʰɔre t͡ʃɔ  igle
am par୍sɔ୍wɔre mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ  tume bɔ୍rah୍mɔɳɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru sɔrɔ୍bɔୋtɔ୍tɔmɔ
ut୍kr̩s୍ʈɔ mukʰia mɔୋ lainɔrɔ kɔmaɳ୍ɖɔୋ
d͡ʒahar nam mũ gɔɳibaku anɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔre tume pɔ୍rɔtʰɔmɔ
tapre b̤is୍mɔ kɔrɔ୍na kɔ୍ripa d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔre b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ
bikɔrɔ୍na ɔsɔwatʰman ehi
sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi sɔ  mɔdɔtɔ୍tiŋ୍kɔ pakʰre ahuri ɔnek b̤aliaɳ୍ʈɔ୍
ebɔŋ t͡ʃes୍ʈa kɔri ehi din mɔribaku pɔ୍rɔsɔ୍tut
mɔୋ paĩ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ rad͡ʒa pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jeke ɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ d̤ɔri
kʰjetre pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek kusɭi | dur୍bɔɭɔmisem୍
amɔrɔ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ dɔrɔ୍sae d͡ʒeũʈʰare b̤is୍mɔ kɔmaɳ୍ɖɔ୍ d̤ɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
ebɔŋ b̤ima taŋ୍kɔ sam୍nare bɔhut sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi
amɔrɔ ɔd̤inajɔkɔmanɔŋɔ୍ku b̤is୍mɔŋɔ୍kɔ nikɔʈɔtɔrɔ hebaku d͡ʒɔtɔ୍nɔban huɔnɔ୍tu
semane kɔɳɔ sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ kɔriparibe bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mɔୋ selku uɖai diɔ 
tapre br̩d୍d̤ɔ rad͡ʒaŋ୍kɔ sɔŋɔ୍ketre
rɔkɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ kɔriba
paĩ t͡ʃit୍kar kɔri siŋhɔrɔ gɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍d͡ʒɔnɔ pɔri gɔɖɔ଼igla
turiʈi mɔhan kɔnɔkɔku bɔ୍le ebɔŋ ehar sɔbɔ୍dɔre
turi ebɔŋ ɖɔ଼୍rɔmɔ୍ sim୍bɔlɔ୍ ebɔŋ gɔŋɔ୍gɔ ebɔŋ siŋ୍gɔ
hɔʈʰat୍ t͡ʃit୍kar kɔla d͡ʒehetu
g̤ur୍ɳɔ୍ɳibɔɭɔjɔrɔ bis୍pʰɔୋrɔɳɔ ehipri ut୍ted͡ʒna dekʰagla
tapre dekʰad͡ʒaipare semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ suna kar upre
d̤ɔɭa g̤ɔୋɖa sɔhit d͡ʒɔୋɖa d͡ʒai semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔsel୍
kr̩s୍ɳɔ b̤ɔgɔban taŋ୍kɔ par୍sɔ୍wɔre ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun
kr̩s୍ɳɔ gɔɳɔ୍ʈʰire tala pɔkai taŋ୍kɔrɔ br̩hɔtɔ୍ sɔŋɔ୍kʰɔku
d͡ʒeɳ୍ʈɔrɔ haɖ kʰɔୋdei kɔritʰile | ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun
in୍dɔ୍rɔŋɔ୍kɔ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ upharɔku uɖ଼aile b̤ima b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ
 gɔd̤iabeli b̤ima ek lɔmɔ୍ba riɖ୍sɔŋɔ୍kʰɔ uɖ଼aila
ebɔŋ d͡ʒud̤is୍ʈʰir kun୍tiŋ୍kɔ dɔୋsɔhin puɔ
ek sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi sel୍ bid͡ʒɔjɔrɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ
ebɔŋ nakula taŋ୍kɔ sɔŋɔ୍kʰɔ upre sɔ୍ril୍ uɖaile
d͡ʒahar nam hela miʈʰa d̤ɔ୍wɔni sahedeb taŋ୍kɔ namit rɔtɔ୍nɔb̤ɔɳɔ୍ɖar
 ebɔŋ taŋ୍kɔ upre kasiŋ୍kɔ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ |
taŋ୍kɔ karre
tʰiba sikʰaɳ୍ɖi d̤ɔ୍ris୍ʈadumɔnɔ୍ biraʈa sɔtɔ୍jɔki ɔnɔ୍sɔbɔɖeɖ୍ dɔ୍rɔ  pɔɖa
taŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit he pr̩tʰibir pɔ୍rɔb̤u
dir୍g̤ɔ sɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ sub̤ɔdɔ୍raŋ୍kɔ pilamane sɔmɔsɔ୍te ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔre uɖ଼igle d͡ʒepri pr̩tʰibi
kɔmɔ୍piba
sɔhɔ bɔd͡ʒɔ୍rɔpat hela । heb̤in୍
tapre dɔ୍wi
d̤r̩tirɔsɔ୍riŋ୍kɔ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ seʈ୍
ɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ d̤ɔnu ɔŋɔ୍kit d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ
tɔtɔkʰjɔɳat୍ b̤aŋ୍gibaɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun d͡ʒahar sɔŋɔ୍ket bɔ୍jad͡ʒ୍
hɔnuman maŋ୍kɔɖɔ଼ tʰila ehi kɔtʰa
kɔ୍ris୍ɳa dib୍jɔ taŋ୍kɔ rɔtʰɔ
ɖɔ୍raib୍̤ ɖauɳ୍ʈɔles୍ kʰɔୋla pɔɖɔ଼iare sɔ 
nɔ୍jɔbahiniku  । 




ehipri ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kɔle he b̤arɔtɔ
hɔୋsɔ୍ʈɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre d͡ʒe sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij rɔtʰɔ
ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ kar t͡ʃɔlaile d͡ʒeũʈʰare kʰjimɔd̤ɔɭa g̤ɔୋɖa
d͡ʒeũʈʰare b̤is୍mɔ netr̩t୍wɔ neitʰile ebɔŋ ɖɔ୍rɔୋna ebɔŋ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤umane |
dekʰ se ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍ku kɔhitʰile d͡ʒeũʈʰare semane ʈʰia huɔnɔ୍ti
tumɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kij kurus୍ ebɔŋ rad͡ʒkumar
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek hatre taŋ୍kɔ g̤ɔrɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kij natuɳi
ebɔŋ sairɔsɔ୍ mamũ ebɔŋ b̤ai o put୍rɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kij
tɔtʰa d͡ʒɔ୍waĩ ebɔŋ b̤ɔɳɔd͡ʒa
saŋ୍gɔ ebɔŋ sɔmɔ୍manit pɔ୍rat͡ʃinmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit mis୍rit  ketek ehi par୍sɔ୍wɔre
au kit͡ʃʰi par୍sɔ୍wɔre rɔhila ebɔŋ birୋd̤ɔ kɔrutʰiba lɔୋkɔŋɔ୍ku dekʰi
ehipri kiʈ୍ sɔtɔ୍ru bɔ  ଼ilaɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍kɔ hr̩dɔjɔ
dɔja sɔhit tɔrɔɭigla d͡ʒetebeɭe se eha kɔhitʰile
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
kr̩s୍ɳɔ mũ dekʰe eʈʰaku as
semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ sad̤arɔɳɔ rɔkɔ୍tɔ  aɭiba paĩ as amɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kijmane
mɔୋrɔ sɔdɔsɔ୍jɔmane bipʰɔɭɔ huɔnɔ୍ti mɔୋ d͡ʒib̤ mɔୋ paʈire sukʰid͡ʒae
ek kɔmɔ୍pɔnɔ mɔୋ sɔrirku rɔୋmaɲ୍t͡ʃɔkɔrɔ kɔre ebɔŋ mɔୋrɔ kes
b̤ɔjɔb̤it hɔୋid͡ʒae mɔୋrɔ dur୍bɔɭɔ hatru
gaɳ୍ɖib୍̤ b̤ɔlɔ d̤ɔnu d͡ʒɔ୍wɔrɔ d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ
kɔre mũ kɔdapi ʈʰia hebi nahĩ
mɔୋ b̤itre d͡ʒibɔnɔ pɔhɔ̃ri dur୍bɔɭɔ mɔne hue
mũ du  kʰɔ o kan୍diba t͡ʃʰɔɖa au kit͡ʃʰi dekʰi nahĩ
he kesɔbɔ eha b̤ɔlɔ nuhẽ
pɔrɔsɔ୍pɔrɔrɔ hɔtɔ୍jaru b̤ɔlɔ kit͡ʃʰi nahĩ
dekʰ mũ bid͡ʒɔjɔ ebɔŋ ad̤ipɔtɔ୍jɔ d̤ɔnɔ ebɔŋ sɔhɔd͡ʒɔtaku g̤r̩ɳa kɔre 
teɳu du  kʰɔrɔ sɔhit d͡ʒitili aha keũ bid͡ʒɔjɔ
anɔnɔ୍dɔ aɳipare gɔୋbin୍da keũ d̤ɔni luʈ
lab̤ kɔriparib keũ nijɔmɔ purɔsɔ୍kar kɔɳɔ bɔ୍jɔbɔd̤an
d͡ʒibɔnɔ nid͡ʒe mɔd̤ur mɔnehue epri rɔkɔ୍tɔ sɔhit kiɳad͡ʒae
emane eʈʰare ʈʰia hɔୋitʰiba dekʰi mɔribaku pɔ୍rɔsɔ୍tut
d͡ʒahaŋ୍kɔ paĩ d͡ʒibɔnɔ nɔ୍jajpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ tʰila ebɔŋ anɔnɔ୍dɔ pɔ୍rɔsɔnɔ୍nɔ hela
ebɔŋ sɔkɔ୍ti bɔhumul୍jɔ hela  gɔ୍raɳ୍ɖejar sair ebɔŋ puɔ
b̤ai sɔ୍wɔsur ebɔŋ putura
pɔ୍rat͡ʃin ebɔŋ bɔnɔ୍d̤ugɔɳɔ
d͡ʒɔdio semane amku maribaku t͡ʃes୍ʈa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti tɔtʰapi mũ emanɔŋɔ୍kɔ upre mr̩t୍jur mukabila kɔribi ki
he mad̤usudɔnɔ gɔୋʈie  ʈɔka nuhẽ  mũ lab̤ kɔribi
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ tinୋʈi d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ nijɔmɔ
tahele par୍tʰib rad͡ʒ୍jɔku ɔkɔ୍tiar kɔriba kete kɔmɔ୍  emanɔŋɔ୍ku hɔtɔ୍ja
kɔriba pɔ୍rɔd͡ʒɔnɔnɔ kin୍tu du  kʰɔ kr̩s୍ɳɔ d͡ʒɔdi semane
dɔୋsi tebe ame semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mr̩t୍ju dɔ୍wara dɔୋsi heba
semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ pap am upre alୋkit heb d͡ʒɔdi ame
d̤r̩tirɔsɔtɔ୍rɔrɔ sehi put୍rɔmanɔŋɔ୍ku ebɔŋ amɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kijmanɔŋɔ୍ku hɔtɔ୍ja kɔriba
he mad̤ɔbɔ setʰiru keũ san୍ti asipare
karɔɳɔ d͡ʒɔdi pɔ୍rɔkr̩tre lɔୋb̤ɔ ebɔŋ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔ dɔ୍wara ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔ hɔୋid͡ʒae
emane dekʰi paribe nahĩ kim୍ba dekʰibe nahĩ
hɔtɔ୍ja kɔrad͡ʒaitʰiba rad͡ʒkij d̤aɖ଼i ebɔŋ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kijmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ pap
am୍b̤emane epri ɔpɔrad̤ru kipri durei rɔhiba ut͡ʃit୍ nuhẽ 
ame d͡ʒeũmane dɔୋsɔ ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔru | ebɔŋ lɔd͡ʒɔ୍d͡ʒa ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔrɔ 
he tume anɔnɔ୍dit d͡ʒɔnar୍dɔna 
g̤ɔrɔguɖ଼iku d̤ɔ୍wɔnsɔ kɔri
semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ mɔd̤ur nirɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ g̤ɔrɔୋi d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ
ebɔnriti ɔbɔheɭit d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ bilup୍tɔ  sehi g̤ɔrɔ upre ɔsub̤ta
pɔ୍rɔbes kɔre
ehar mɔhiɭamane ɔbibahit huɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒeũʈʰaru bɔsɔnɔ୍tɔ
pagɔɭɔ abeg ebɔŋ d͡ʒatir mis୍rɔɳɔ
sehi pɔribarku ek nɔrɔ୍kɔwar୍ɖɔ ras୍ta pɔʈʰaiba
ebɔŋ d͡ʒie dus୍ʈɔ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔ dɔ୍wara ehar binas kɔla |
na ebɔŋ sɔmɔ୍manit pitr̩purusɔŋɔ୍kɔ at୍ma
​​semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ san୍ti sɔ୍tʰanru kʰɔsi pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti
ɔnɔ୍tim sɔnsɔ୍karpiʈʰa ebɔŋ mr̩t୍jud͡ʒɔɭɔru bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃit huɔnɔ୍ti |  # 
teɳu amɔrɔ pɔbit୍rɔ b̤ɔd͡ʒɔnɔ sikʰja diɔ | ehipri d͡ʒɔdi ame
par୍tʰib sɔkɔ୍ti pɔ୍rem paĩ kin୍sɔpʰɔୋlɔ୍kɔ ebɔŋ saŋ୍gɔmanɔŋɔ୍ku hɔtɔ୍ja kɔru
ɔhɔୋb̤aʈ eha kete kʰɔrap dɔୋsɔ tʰila
mũ eha b̤ɔlɔ bɔୋli mɔne kɔre d͡ʒɔdi mɔୋrɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kijmane ag̤at kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
semanɔŋɔ୍ku ɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔhin sam୍na kɔribaku ebɔŋ mɔୋ sɔ୍tɔnɔku
sapʰ୍ʈɔ ebɔŋ bɔrɔ୍t͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃʰa bɔhɔnɔ kɔribaku  ʈɔka sɔhit ut୍tɔrɔ deba ɔpekʰja |
ɔteb sehi dui hɔୋsɔ୍ʈɔŋɔ୍kɔ sam୍nare
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun taŋ୍kɔ rɔtʰɔ asɔnɔre buɖ଼igle
ebɔŋ hr̩dɔjɔre ɔsus୍tʰɔ hɔୋi d̤ɔnu o tir pɔɖɔ଼ibaku diɔnɔ୍tu।
b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍gita rɔ ses ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ehar
nam ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunbisad
kim୍ba ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍kɔ du  kʰɔrɔ pus୍tɔkɔ।




ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj 
sɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔjɔ |
se epri kɔruɳa ebɔŋ epri du  kʰɔre pɔripur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ
akʰiru luhɔlɔhɔri hɔtas kɔʈʰɔୋrɔ sɔbɔ୍dɔre
ɖɔ୍raib̤ɔrɔ mɔd̤usudɔnɔ ehipri sɔmɔ୍bɔୋd̤it kɔle
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
ehi dur୍bɔɭɔta tumku kemiti neit͡ʃʰi keũʈʰaru
 rɔɳa nir୍bɔୋd̤ɔ ɔsubid̤a sahsimanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ lɔd͡ʒɔ୍d͡ʒad͡ʒɔnɔkɔ
guɳɔrɔ pɔtʰɔku barɔɳɔ kɔre na ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun
nid͡ʒku dur୍bɔɭɔta paĩ barɔɳɔ kɔrɔ eha tumɔrɔ d͡ʒɔୋdɔ୍d̤a namku mar୍sɔ kɔre
 b̤ɔjɔb̤it pʰiʈ
d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ huɔ nid͡ʒe huɔ uʈʰ tum୍b̤ɔrɔ sɔtɔ୍rugɔɳɔ
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
mũ kipri d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔre
b̤is୍mɔ kim୍ba ɖɔ୍rɔୋnahe pɔ୍rɔd̤anɔŋɔ୍kɔ upre sapʰ୍ʈɔ sɔhit guɭi t͡ʃɔɭaibi 
ub̤ɔjɔ pud͡ʒɔkɔ ub̤ɔjɔ sɔmɔ୍manɔd͡ʒɔnɔkɔ bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti
b̤ikariŋ୍kɔ ruʈire bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃiba b̤ɔlɔ
 d͡ʒeũmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit ame d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ b̤ɔlɔpau
sɔmr̩d୍d̤ɔ b̤ɔୋd͡ʒire semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ rɔkɔ୍tɔrɔ sɔ୍wad ɔpekʰja
ebɔŋ dɔୋsɔre bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔnɔ୍tu
a  eha ɔd̤ik kʰɔrap tʰilakie d͡ʒaɳe 
b̤ik୍ʈɔrɔ heba kim୍ba eʈʰare pɔrad͡ʒit heba
d͡ʒetebeɭe semane kɔ୍rɔୋd̤it b̤abre am sɔhit muhãmuhĩ huɔnɔ୍ti
kahar mr̩t୍ju sɔ୍wɔpɔ୍nɔku bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃaitʰae
dɔja hɔd͡ʒigla sɔnɔ୍deh dɔ୍  ara
mɔୋrɔ t͡ʃin୍tad̤arabib୍̤ran୍tɔ
tumku gaiɖ୍ mũ ɔd̤ik sɔmɔ୍man kɔre
d͡ʒaha dɔ୍  ara mũ sikʰibaku pɔramɔrɔ୍sɔ deipare
mũ d͡ʒaɳe nahĩ
pɔ୍raɳ ebɔŋ b̤abnare d͡ʒɔɭid͡ʒaitʰiba du  kʰɔ kɔɳɔ b̤ɔlɔ kɔrib
d͡ʒɔdi mũ pr̩tʰibir ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij mukʰ୍jɔ 
ek  sɔ୍wɔrɔ  ebɔŋ emane seʈʰaru t͡ʃaligle
sɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔjɔ |
teɳu ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒunɔŋɔ୍ku pɔ୍rɔb̤uŋ୍kɔ hr̩dɔjɔre kɔhila
ebɔŋ dir୍g̤ɔ nis୍bas t͡ʃʰaɖi kɔhila mũ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ kɔribi nahĩ setebeɭe t͡ʃup୍ rɔhile |
kahaku kɔୋmɔɭɔ hɔsɔ sɔhit he b̤arɔtɔ
d͡ʒetebeɭe rad͡ʒkumar hɔtas hɔୋi sehi hɔୋsɔ୍ʈɔguɖikɔrɔ dɔ୍wiguɳit kan୍dile
kr̩s୍ɳɔ  sɔ୍wɔrij pɔdɔre ut୍tɔrɔ dele
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
tume du  kʰɔ kɔrɔ d͡ʒeũʈʰare kɔ  ɳɔsi du  kʰɔ rɔhiba ut͡ʃit୍ nuhẽ tume d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ
sɔbɔ୍dɔ kɔhut͡ʃʰ hr̩dɔjɔrɔ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanimane
d͡ʒibit kim୍ba mr̩t୍jubɔrɔɳɔ kɔrutʰiba lɔୋkɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ sɔୋkɔ kɔrɔ nahĩ।
na mũ na tume kim୍ba emanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru kɔ ɳɔsi
kebe nuhẽ kim୍ba kebebi rɔhib nahĩ
t͡ʃirkaɭ paĩ ebɔŋ pɔre |
sɔmɔsɔ୍te bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔnɔ୍ti sɔrɔ୍bɔda bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔnɔ୍ti mɔɳisɔrɔ pʰɔ୍rem୍ ku
d͡ʒepri sisu ebɔŋ d͡ʒɔ  bɔnɔ ebɔŋ bɔjɔsɔ ase sehipri ɔnɔ୍jɔ ebɔŋ ɔnɔ୍jan୍jɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔbasɔsɔ୍tʰanɔrɔ
raid͡ʒiŋɔpɔ୍ ​​ebɔŋ leʈiɳɖaun୍ as  d͡ʒaha d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanimane d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ b̤ɔjɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ | eha tumɔrɔ in୍dɔ୍rij  tumɔrɔ in୍dɔ୍rijd͡ʒibɔnɔ ​​upadanguɖik paĩ rɔୋmaɲ୍t͡ʃɔkɔrɔ  tumku ut୍tap ebɔŋ tʰɔɳɔ୍ɖa du  kʰɔ ebɔŋ anɔnɔ୍dɔ aɳiba eha sɔŋkʰjip୍tɔ ebɔŋ pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔsiɭ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ





d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani b̤alu pɔri | d͡ʒeũ at୍ma ​​g̤uɲ୍t͡ʃi nɔtʰae
pɔ୍raɳ d͡ʒaha ek dr̩  ebɔŋ nirɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ san୍tɔ sɔhit
du  kʰɔ kɔre ebɔŋ udasin b̤abre anɔnɔ୍dɔ nie
 d͡ʒibɔnɔre ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij d͡ʒaha d͡ʒaha heba
bɔnɔ୍dɔ hɔୋiparib nahĩ d͡ʒaha nahĩ
taha bid୍jɔman rɔhib nahĩ | ub̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ ehi sɔtɔ୍jɔku dekʰiba
heut͡ʃʰi semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒeũmane dur୍g̤ɔʈɔɳaru muɭ ɔnsɔ
t͡ʃʰairu pɔdar୍tʰɔ | ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij
sikʰ d͡ʒibɔnɔ heut͡ʃʰi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍kɔ mad୍̤jɔmɔre d͡ʒibɔnɔ bis୍tar kɔre
eha kɔ  ɳɔsi sɔ୍tʰanre kɔ  ɳɔsi upajre hɔୋiparib nahĩ
d͡ʒek  ɳɔsi pɔ୍rɔkare hɔ୍ras huɔ ruh kim୍ba pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔ hɔୋiparib nahĩ |
kin୍tu ehi kʰjɔɳɔsɔ୍tʰaji pʰɔ୍rem୍ paĩ d͡ʒaha
at୍ma ​​sɔhit mr̩t୍juhin ɔsim ɔsim sɔhit sut͡ʃit kɔre
semane binɔsɔ୍ʈɔ huɔnɔ୍ti | semane binɔsɔ୍ʈɔ huɔnɔ୍tu rad͡ʒkumar ebɔŋ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ kɔrɔ
d͡ʒie kɔhib dekʰ mũ d͡ʒɔɳe lɔୋkɔŋɔ୍ku hɔtɔ୍ja kɔrit͡ʃʰi
d͡ʒie b̤abib dekʰ mũ nihɔtɔ se duhẽ
kit͡ʃʰi d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ d͡ʒibɔnɔ hɔtɔ୍ja kɔriparib nahĩ | d͡ʒibɔnɔ nihɔtɔ nuhẽ
at୍ma ​​kebe d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ hɔୋintʰile at୍ma ​​kɔdapi bɔnɔ୍dɔ heb nahĩ
eha kebe nuhẽ ses ebɔŋ arɔmɔ୍b̤ɔ heut͡ʃʰi sɔ୍wɔpɔ୍nɔ
d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔhin ebɔŋ mr̩t୍juhin ebɔŋ pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔsiɭ at୍ma ​​t͡ʃirdin paĩ rɔhitʰae
mr̩t୍ju ehaku ad t͡ʃʰuĩ nahĩ mr̩t d͡ʒɔdio ehar g̤ɔrɔ dekʰad͡ʒae
kie d͡ʒaɳe d͡ʒe eha nirɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ at୍mɔnir୍b̤ɔrɔsiɭ
ɔmɔrɔ ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij  epri
kɔhib ki mũ d͡ʒɔɳe bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍tiŋ୍ku hɔtɔ୍ja kɔrit͡ʃʰi kim୍ba hɔtɔ୍ja kɔrit͡ʃʰi
na kin୍tu d͡ʒetebeɭe d͡ʒɔɳe
nid͡ʒɔrɔ puruɳa pɔୋsakku t͡ʃʰɔɖɔ଼ai die

mũ ad͡ʒi ehaku pin୍d̤ibi

ek basɔsɔ୍tʰan paibaku pas୍ kɔre |

kim୍ba sukʰila pɔbɔnɔ sukʰid͡ʒae nahĩ |

 gɔୋʈie bid୍jɔman at୍ma ​​ tume kan୍dib ki

। d͡ʒaha g̤ɔʈut͡ʃʰi
d͡ʒaha ɔnɔ୍jɔtʰa hɔୋipare nahĩ
d͡ʒibɔd͡ʒɔnɔ୍tumanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲatre ase mr̩t୍ju
ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲatre ase semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre pɔ୍raɳimane ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
pɔ୍rij pɔ୍rin୍sɔ eʈʰare kɔɳɔ du  kʰɔ ɔt͡ʃʰi
t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar t͡ʃɔtur t͡ʃin୍ta kɔribaku

pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jekɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔmɔjɔ sɔ୍rɔbɔɳɔ
mɔnus୍jɔ eha mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒaɳe nahĩ eha dekʰiba kete as୍t͡ʃɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔd͡ʒɔnɔkɔ
d͡ʒetebeɭe dekʰiba kɔhiba ebɔŋ suɳiba sɔmap୍tɔ hue

। tumɔrɔ ɔnsɔ kɔrɔ
nid͡ʒ nam pɔ୍rɔti d̤ɔ୍jan diɔ ebɔŋ kɔmɔ୍pit huɔ nahĩ ainɔgɔtɔ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ ɔpekʰja
samrik pɔ୍raɳku b̤ɔlɔ kɔripare nahĩ

 gɔ  rɔbɔmɔjɔ ebɔŋ nɔ୍jajd͡ʒuk୍tɔ ɔbaɲ୍t͡ʃʰit taŋ୍kɔ paĩ

। kin୍tu kukʰ୍jat kʰɔrap

purୋhitɔŋɔ୍kɔ dɔ୍wara au ɔsubid̤are pɔɖɔ଼ile nahĩ
eha nirapɔdɔre bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃib ebɔŋ nis୍t͡ʃit heb
d̤ɔ୍janre sɔ୍tʰir hɔୋi bɔŋɔ୍ka | eha heut͡ʃʰi d͡ʒɔୋgɔ  ebɔŋ san୍ti
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
taŋ୍kɔrɔ t͡ʃih୍nɔ kɔɳɔ d͡ʒie sehi sɔ୍tʰir hr̩dɔjɔ
pɔbit୍rɔ d̤ɔ୍janre nis୍t͡ʃit hɔୋit͡ʃʰi
kesab̤a ame taŋ୍kɔ b̤asɔɳɔ kipri d͡ʒaɳiba se bɔsit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti se
ɔnɔ୍jɔ purusmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔri gɔti kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
d͡ʒetebeɭe d͡ʒɔɳe pɔ୍ritaŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ
it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰaku pɔrit୍jag kɔre d͡ʒaha mɔnɔku hɔlaitʰae 
taŋ୍kɔ pɔ୍raɳre taŋ୍kɔ at୍ma ​​paĩ sɔmɔ୍pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ aram paitʰae
se d͡ʒɔୋgɔ pɔ୍rap୍tɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti  sehi bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti epri
du  kʰɔre hɔtas nuhẽ ebɔŋ anɔnɔ୍dɔre
ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik anɔnɔ୍dit nuhẽ
abeg b̤ɔjɔ ebɔŋ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔrɔ t͡ʃap bahare bas kɔriba  san୍tɔre sɔ୍tʰir hɔୋit͡ʃʰi
ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ t͡ʃin୍tad̤arar  ehipri d͡ʒɔɳe
muni sed͡ʒ୍ pɔ୍rɔkr̩t rik୍lus୍
d͡ʒie
mansɔrɔ bɔnɔ୍d̤ɔnɔ dɔ୍wara mɔnɔ୍dɔ d͡ʒinis ebɔŋ b̤ɔlɔku nie ki nirasa
kim୍ba anɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔre nahĩ epri
b̤alu d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ sɔ୍pɔsɔ୍ʈɔ t͡ʃih୍nɔ d͡ʒie t͡ʃit୍rɔ kɔrib
d͡ʒepri d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani kĩt͡ʃʰɔ ehar t͡ʃari padku surkʰjit b̤abre
nid͡ʒ  al tɔɭe ʈaɳib taŋ୍kɔrɔ paɲ୍t͡ʃɔʈi dur୍bɔɭɔ in୍dɔ୍rijguɖik |
duniaru at୍maŋ୍kɔ bɔkɔlɔrɔ୍ tɔɭe
d͡ʒaha ɔnɔ୍jɔmanɔŋɔ୍ku ak୍rɔmɔɳɔ kɔre epri d͡ʒɔɳe mɔୋrɔ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ t͡ʃih୍nɔ ɔt͡ʃʰi ki d͡ʒinisguɖik d͡ʒaha bu 
ae at୍mɔsasitru durei ruh na eha ase
d͡ʒie
bidaj bahare rɔhe tar b̤ɔୋkɔ au d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ hela nahĩ | tɔtʰapi eha sud͡ʒୋgɔ heu
he kun୍tir put୍rɔ d͡ʒe ek sasit mɔnɔ
kit͡ʃʰi sɔmɔjɔ in୍dɔ୍rij  ɖɔ଼ku ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔrib ebɔŋ
muɭ dɔ୍wara dr̩  at୍mɔ nijɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔɳɔku lɔ  ei kɔrib | se punɔrɔ୍bar
taŋ୍kɔrɔ rad͡ʒ୍jɔ pʰeri paibaku diɔnɔ୍tu se ehaku pɔras୍tɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍tu ebɔŋ
mɔୋ ud୍des୍jɔre bɔsɔnɔ୍tu | sehi bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti kebɔɭɔ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani
d͡ʒie nid͡ʒ upre dɔkʰjɔta rɔkʰe d͡ʒɔdi
ɔrɔ୍tʰɔrɔ bɔsɔ୍tuguɖ଼ik upre gɔୋʈie t͡ʃin୍ta kɔre seʈʰare
akɔrɔ୍sɔɳɔ  rɔɳa akɔrɔ୍sɔɳɔru it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa bɔ e
pɔ୍rɔbɔɭɔ abeg paĩ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ୍tɔ abeg
beprua tapre sɔ୍mr̩ti  sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ bis୍wasg̤atɔkɔta 
ut୍tɔmɔ ud୍des୍jɔku d͡ʒibaku diɔ ebɔŋ mɔnɔku nɔsɔ୍ʈɔ kɔridie
d͡ʒepɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ ud୍des୍jɔ mɔnɔ ebɔŋ mɔnus୍jɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ɔnabɔsɔ୍jɔkɔ |
kin୍tu d͡ʒɔdi d͡ʒɔɳe ɔrɔ୍tʰɔrɔ bɔsɔ୍tuguɖ଼ik sɔhit karbar kɔre
pɔ୍rem kɔre nahĩ ebɔŋ g̤r̩ɳa kɔre nahĩ semanɔŋɔ୍ku semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ
muk୍tɔ pɔ୍raɳɔrɔ seba kɔrɔ d͡ʒaha ɔtisɔjɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u
lɔୋ epri lɔୋkɔ san୍tɔ hue
ebɔŋ sehi san୍tiru uʈʰib
taŋ୍kɔ par୍tʰib d͡ʒɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔɳar ses ebɔŋ arୋgɔ୍jɔ
d͡ʒehetu sasit it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa at୍maku san୍tire rɔkʰe |
ɔbib̤ɔkɔ୍tɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ at୍ma ​​taŋ୍kɔrɔ nuhẽ
kim୍ba se nid͡ʒ bisɔjɔre d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ d͡ʒahar ɔb̤ab
san୍ti kipri bɔ  e ebɔŋ se eha t͡ʃahãnɔ୍ti
se keũʈʰaru sukʰ paĩ b̤ɔrɔsa kɔribe
mɔnɔ
d͡ʒaha nid͡ʒku ɔnub̤ɔbɔrɔ sɔୋ ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔribaku die
ehar d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ helɔmɔ୍ dur hɔୋid͡ʒae
ebɔŋ g̤ur୍ɳɔ୍ɳibat୍ja tɔrɔŋɔ୍gɔre d͡ʒahad͡ʒ pɔri
d̤ɔ୍wɔnsɔ ebɔŋ mr̩t୍juku t͡ʃɔɭaitʰae | kebɔɭɔ taŋ୍kɔ sɔhit mɔhan pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
d͡ʒahar in୍dɔ୍rijguɖik bud୍d̤iman d͡ʒinis dɔ୍wara pɔ୍rɔb̤abit hue nahĩ 
kebɔɭɔ d͡ʒie taŋ୍kɔ dɔkʰjɔta d̤ɔritʰae
d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanku sid୍d̤ɔ dekʰae | mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔrat୍riɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar kɔɳɔ
ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲat at୍maŋ୍kɔ paĩ d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ din
taŋ୍kɔ sɔ୍wɔt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃʰɔ dr̩s୍ʈire d͡ʒaha d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ din pɔri dekʰad͡ʒae
 rati paĩ ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲɔtar g̤ɔnɔ rati
taŋ୍kɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔkr̩t dekʰutʰiba akʰi paĩ d͡ʒɔɳasuɳa | se heut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti sɔnɔ୍tʰɔ
ebɔŋ sɔmud୍rɔ pɔri dinku din
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ desru bɔnɔ୍ja pɔris୍tʰiti gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔre d͡ʒaha
ehar simaku kebe bi pɔ୍rɔbahit kɔre nahĩ ebɔŋ
nɔdiguɖ଼ik dɔ୍  ara pʰeɖ୍ hue nahĩ kin୍tu sehimanɔŋɔ୍kɔ dɔ୍  ara ɔsurkʰjit 
sehipri upd͡ʒuk୍tɔ taŋ୍kɔ pɔ୍raɳɔrɔ sɔmud୍rɔku
d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan d͡ʒɔgɔtɔ d͡ʒadukɔrɔ  rɔɳa  aɭe
semane d͡ʒepri paile taŋ୍ku t͡ʃʰaɖi t͡ʃalid͡ʒaan୍ti bina
sɔ୍rɔdɔ୍d̤are kin୍tu ɔbɔsis୍ʈɔ sɔmud୍rɔ |
hɔ̃ d͡ʒie mansɔrɔ d͡ʒuaɭi hɔlai
pɔ୍rɔb̤u sebɔkɔ nuhẽ nid͡ʒɔrɔ lɔୋb̤ɔru bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃe
gɔrɔ୍bɔru abegru at୍mɔ rɔ papru muk୍tɔ kɔrɔ san୍tir
san୍ti he pɔ୍ritʰaŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ
taha heut͡ʃʰi bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍mɔrɔ rad͡ʒ୍jɔ seʈʰare kɔ  ɳɔsi b̤ɔjɔ nahĩ
d͡ʒetebeɭe sehi ses pɔdɔkʰjepʈi pɔhɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃe se d͡ʒeũʈʰare rɔhibe seʈʰare
ruh d͡ʒetebeɭe se mɔribe ehipri sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sɔmɔtɔɭɔ sɔ୍tʰanru
nir୍baɳ b̤ɔgɔbanɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit nir୍baɳku bɔ୍las୍ʈɔ kɔribaku |
eʈʰare ses ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj  | b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍gita d͡ʒahar nam
sad୍̤jad͡ʒୋgɔ
kim୍ba buk୍ ɔpʰɔ୍ ɖɔkɔ୍ʈɔ୍rin୍sɔ |




ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj 
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
tume d͡ʒahaku sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ mɔɳis pɔ୍rɔsɔnsa kɔrɔ d͡ʒɔnar୍dɔ୍dɔnɔ
d͡ʒɔdi d̤ɔ୍jan
kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ ɔpekʰja ek ut୍tɔmɔ d͡ʒinis ɔʈe tebe mɔhan kesab̤a
tume mɔୋte ehi b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔre bad୍̤jɔ kɔrɔ ki
bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mũ tumɔrɔ sɔnɔ୍dehɔd͡ʒɔnɔkɔ bɔkɔ୍tɔbɔ୍jɔre bit͡ʃɭit
mɔୋte gɔୋʈie kɔtʰa kuh ebɔŋ mɔୋte nis୍t͡ʃit kuh
keũ ras୍tare mũ b̤ɔlɔ ses paibi
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
mũ tum୍b̤ɔku kɔhili nirih pɔ୍rɔb̤u
ehi duniaku duiʈi pɔtʰɔ pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sit hɔୋit͡ʃʰi d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ duiʈi bid୍jaɭɔjɔ |
pɔ୍rɔtʰɔme
saŋ୍kia d͡ʒaha kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ ɔnud͡ʒaji sɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔjɔ kɔre
 #  karɔɳɔ ɔnud͡ʒaji pɔrɔbɔrɔ୍tɔ୍ti d͡ʒɔୋgɔ d͡ʒaha
d̤ɔ୍jan dɔ୍wara pɔ୍rap୍tɔ hue ad୍̤jat୍mik b̤abre
tɔtʰapi eguɖ଼ik gɔୋʈie kɔ  ɳɔsi bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔru durei rɔhibe nahĩ
 na ebɔŋ kehi
sid୍d̤ɔtaku tɔ୍jag kɔri asibe nahĩ | na ebɔŋ sɔmɔjɔrɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi d͡ʒɔʈɔ୍ d͡ʒek
 ɳɔsi sɔmɔjɔre kɔ  ɳɔsi kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔku binas kɔre
taŋ୍kɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir nijɔmɔ
taŋ୍ku it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa kɔre nahĩ
karɔɳɔ t͡ʃin୍tad̤ara kɔɭɔ୍pɔnare kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔre d͡ʒie
mansɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔku dɔmɔnɔ kɔribaku bɔsitʰae
tɔtʰapi se nid͡ʒ nis୍kɔ୍rij hr̩dɔjɔre semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ bisɔjɔre t͡ʃin୍ta kɔri
ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲɔ ebɔŋ dɔୋsi kɔpɔʈi kʰeɭɔnɔ୍ti
kin୍tu d͡ʒie
dr̩  sɔrir sɔhit mɔnɔ seba kɔre se nid͡ʒɔrɔ mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔ sɔkɔ୍tiku d͡ʒɔୋgɔ୍jɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre sɔmɔrɔ୍pɔɳɔ kɔre
lab̤ kʰɔୋd͡ʒunahĩ ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun epri d͡ʒɔɳe
sɔmɔ୍manɔd͡ʒɔnɔkɔ | tumɔrɔ bɔɳɔ୍ʈit kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔrɔ
kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ nis୍kɔ୍rijta ɔpekʰja ɔd̤ik ut୍kr̩s୍ʈɔ
sɔrirɔrɔ ɔb̤ab kam ɔb̤abru agku bɔ e nahĩ |
pɔbit୍rɔtar ek kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ ɔt͡ʃʰi
bis୍wɔban୍d̤utʰiba pɔris୍rɔmɔ pɔri d͡ʒaha
bis୍wɔsɔ୍tɔ at୍maku ban୍d̤e nahĩ ehipri par୍tʰib kɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔbɔ୍jɔ
it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰaru muk୍tɔ kɔrɔ ebɔŋ tume
tumɔrɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij ud୍des୍jɔku b̤ɔlɔ b̤abre kɔrib | pɔ୍rɔd͡ʒapti kuhɔnɔ୍tu
 arɔmɔ୍b̤ɔre d͡ʒetebeɭe sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ mɔnus୍jɔ sr̩s୍ʈi hela
ebɔŋ manɔbɔd͡ʒati sɔhit bɔɭidan  eha kɔrɔ
kam kɔrɔ bɔɭidan bɔɭi
sɔhit br̩d୍d̤i kɔrɔ ebɔŋ bɔ  ଼ eha kamaɖuk୍ heb
tumɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔt͡ʃur ga  deb | tar dug୍d̤ɔku pʰerai
diɔ।
debtamane tum୍b̤ɔku ɔnug୍rɔhɔ pɔ୍rɔdan kɔribe। sehi mansɔguɖ଼ik tume it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa kɔrut͡ʃʰ
debtamane sɔ୍rɔmɔku debe d͡ʒetebeɭe eha
d͡ʒɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲɔbedire dɔsɔmansɔ deb | kin୍tu d͡ʒɔdi kehi pr̩tʰibir pʰɔɭɔ kʰae
 dɔjakri sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔku
kɔ  ɳɔsi pɔris୍rɔmɔrɔ uphar die nahĩ tebe sehi t͡ʃɔୋrɔ taŋ୍kɔ d͡ʒɔgɔtɔru t͡ʃɔୋri kɔre |
d͡ʒeũmane bɔɭidan pɔre kʰad୍jɔ kʰaan୍ti
 semane dɔୋsɔ t͡ʃʰaɖitʰan୍ti kin୍tu d͡ʒeũmane nid͡ʒ paĩ ek b̤ɔୋd͡ʒi bis୍tar
kɔrɔnɔ୍ti semane pap kʰaan୍ti ebɔŋ papɔrɔ pan kɔrɔnɔ୍ti |
kʰad୍jɔ dɔ୍wara d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibit kʰad୍jɔ bɔrɔ୍saʈʰaru ase
ebɔŋ d̤ar୍mik bɔɭidan dɔ୍wara bɔrɔ୍sa ase
ebɔŋ pɔris୍rɔmɔrɔ dɔsɔmansɔ sɔhit bɔɭi diad͡ʒae
ehipri kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maŋ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒie ek
ekmat୍rɔ sɔrɔ୍bɔbɔ୍japi sɔbu sɔmɔjɔre
bɔɭidanre upɔsɔ୍tʰit huɔ | d͡ʒie nibr̩t୍tɔ
hue ehi mɔhan duniar gɔɖɔ଼utʰiba t͡ʃɔkɔku sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ kɔriba paĩ
taŋ୍kɔrɔ ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲan b̤abnaku gɔ୍luʈ୍ kɔri hɔd͡ʒid͡ʒaitʰiba d͡ʒibɔnɔ bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃitʰae
lɔd͡ʒɔ୍d͡ʒad͡ʒɔnɔkɔ ebɔŋ br̩tʰa | nid͡ʒ paĩ bid୍jɔman
at୍mekag୍rɔ ekaki seba kɔriba
taŋ୍kɔrɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi ɔnsɔ nahĩ kit͡ʃʰi hasɔlɔ kɔrad͡ʒai nahĩ
kɔ  ɳɔsi kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kim୍ba ɔnabɔsɔ୍jɔkɔ taŋ୍ku sɔ୍pɔrɔ୍sɔ kɔre nahĩ b̤ɔrɔsa nahĩ
pr̩tʰibir sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibɔd͡ʒɔnɔ୍tuŋ୍kɔ paĩ sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ
taŋ୍kɔʈʰaru nir୍b̤ɔrɔ
kɔre । kebɔɭɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ dɔ୍wara d͡ʒɔnɔkɔ ebɔŋ pɔ୍rat͡ʃin sad̤umane asir୍bad pɔ୍rap୍tɔ hele ɔd̤ikɔnɔ୍tu tumɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔkarɔrɔ sɔmɔrɔ୍tʰɔnɔ paĩ tume aliŋ୍gɔnɔ kɔriba ut͡ʃit୍ | d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanimane d͡ʒaha bat͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti taha ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲan lɔୋkɔmane gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti b̤ɔlɔ lɔୋkɔmane kɔɳɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒɔnɔta ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔribe | he pɔ୍ritʰa put୍rɔ  mɔୋte dekʰ  tinୋʈi pɔ୍rɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ duniare mũ kɔ  ɳɔsi pɔris୍rɔmɔre bɔnɔ୍d̤a nuhẽ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔta mapibaku ɔpekʰja kɔre kɔ  ɳɔsi uphar paibaku baki rɔhila nahĩ tɔtʰapi mũ eʈʰare kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔre ebɔŋ d͡ʒɔdi mũ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔri nɔ tʰili  an୍tɔrik ebɔŋ d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ  d͡ʒeũmane mɔୋte dekʰɔnɔ୍ti |












mar୍gɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ paĩ punɔrɔ୍bar
sɔ୍lɔୋtʰɔku buɖ଼id͡ʒiba karɔɳɔ mũ sɔୋipɖitʰili b̤ɔlɔru hɔ୍ras paibi
ebɔŋ mũ pr̩tʰibir ades b̤aŋ୍gi
tar sɔnɔ୍tanmanɔŋɔ୍ku d̤ɔ୍wɔnsɔ kɔribaku b̤ɔrɔtɔ
ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲat pɔris୍rɔmɔ pɔri bu  iba paĩ bibah
teɳu d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔpɔ୍rap୍tɔ pɔris୍rɔmɔku b̤abmuk୍tɔ hebaku diɔ kin୍tu
d͡ʒɔgɔtɔku ud୍d̤ar ebɔŋ ehar sukʰ aɳibaku sɔ୍tʰir kɔrɔ
sehi sɔrɔɭɔ bɔ୍jɔsɔ୍tɔ hr̩dɔjɔre buɳiba nuhẽ
nirasar bid͡ʒ | hɔ̃
pɔ୍ret୍jɔkɔkɔ elak nid͡ʒɔrɔ ɔnsɔ gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔriba ut͡ʃit୍।
pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ dɔ୍wara sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒinis sɔbuʈʰare
ɔt͡ʃʰi guɳguɖ଼ikɔrɔ parɔsɔ୍pɔrik kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre |
mur୍kʰɔ nid͡ʒku pɔ୍rɔtarɳa kɔri b̤abɔnɔ୍ti mũ eha kɔritʰili
ebɔŋ d͡ʒaha mũ kɔritʰili kin୍tu  a  tume sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi sɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ

in୍dɔ୍rij d͡ʒɔgɔtɔre dr̩s୍jɔman d͡ʒinisguɖik
ebɔŋ guɳguɖik kipri d͡ʒɔୋgɔ୍jɔ heba abɔsɔ୍jɔkɔ
taŋ୍kɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔru mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ durei ruhɔnɔ୍ti | pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir
mar୍gɔ d͡ʒaɳintʰiba
sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ lɔkʰjɔ୍jɔguɖik ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲat d̤ir ebɔŋ nir୍bɔୋd̤ɔ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit mis୍rit |
sehi lɔୋkɔmane tum୍b̤ɔku  uɳ୍ʈi pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti nahĩ।
kin୍tu tumɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ dej ɖist͡ʃar୍d͡ʒɔ mɔୋ sɔpɔkʰjɔre
d̤ɔ୍janku b̤itɔrɔrɔ ken୍dɔ୍rɔ kɔri kɔ
 ɳɔsi lab̤ kʰɔୋd͡ʒu nahĩ sɔnɔ୍tus୍ʈɔ san୍tɔ
isu bihin  d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ d͡ʒeũmane
ehipri b̤abre mɔୋrɔ nijɔmɔ paɭɔnɔ kɔribe d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani ebɔŋ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰasɔkɔ୍tɔ hr̩dɔjɔ
semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔru tɔ୍jag kɔribe
kin୍tu d͡ʒeũmane mɔୋrɔ nijɔmɔku ɔbɔmanna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
b̤abɔnɔ୍ti semane d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti kit͡ʃʰi d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ ebɔŋ kʰjɔtig୍rɔsɔ୍tɔ huɔnɔ୍ti
dɔ୍wɔnɔ୍dɔ୍wɔre ebɔŋ mur୍kʰɔ | sɔୋtʰɔ୍ nir୍dɔ୍desit |
taŋ୍ku ɔd̤ik pʰiʈ୍ kɔrutʰiba ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔri taŋ୍kɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔkarɔrɔ
ebɔŋ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔ୍rɔkarɔrɔ nim୍nɔ pɔ୍raɳi nirɔrɔ୍tʰɔkɔ
nijɔmɔku lab̤ kɔriba | eha abɔsɔ୍jɔkɔ heba abɔsɔ୍jɔkɔ
ɔrɔ୍tʰɔrɔ bɔsɔ୍tuguɖ଼ik ehi b̤abnaku
pɔsɔnɔ୍dɔ ebɔŋ napɔsɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔribaku ut୍sahit kɔrib tɔtʰapi d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanban bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti
emanɔŋɔ୍ku nuhẽ semanɔŋɔ୍ku sɔtɔ୍ru b̤abre d͡ʒaɳitʰae |
pɔrisesre eha b̤ɔlɔ d͡ʒe d͡ʒɔɳe
nid͡ʒ nid͡ʒɔrɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔriparɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒɔdio se bipʰɔɭɔ huɔnɔ୍ti
kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔguɖik nid͡ʒe nuhẽ d͡ʒɔdio semane b̤ɔlɔ mɔne kɔrɔnɔ୍ti |
kɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔbɔ୍jɔ paɭɔnɔ kɔriba mɔriba kɔ  ɳɔsi ɔsus୍tʰɔ nuhẽ
kin୍tu d͡ʒie ɔnɔ୍jɔ ras୍ta kʰɔୋd͡ʒib se epɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ bulib।
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
tɔtʰapi mɔୋte kuh guru mɔnus୍jɔ keũ bɔɭɔ dɔ୍wara
nid͡ʒ ɔsus୍tʰɔtaku d͡ʒae sɔte d͡ʒepri d͡ʒɔɳe

kama eha
ut୍sah ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkarru d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ
d͡ʒaha taŋ୍ku ʈʰelidie | b̤ɔୋkɔrɔ sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi
papi ebɔŋ sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi eha  mɔɳisɔrɔ sɔtɔ୍ru
d̤uã d̤ɔɭa niãku uɖ଼aila b̤ɔɭi
mɔŋɔ୍gɔɭɔ gɔ୍rɔhɔrɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ dɔrɔ୍pɔɳɔ gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔ gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔsɔ୍tʰɔ sisur t͡ʃɔtur୍dɔ୍digre d͡ʒepri
d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mit sisu sehipri d͡ʒinis d͡ʒɔgɔtɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ
dur୍bɔɭɔ miɭa mansɔrɔ ehi it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰare abɔdɔ୍d̤ɔ |
d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani pɔtɔnɔ etʰire d̤ɔrapɖigɔla ɔsɔ୍tʰir sɔtɔ୍ru
eha d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ rup pin୍d̤i
nɔ୍jajd͡ʒuk୍tɔ kin୍tu pɔ୍rɔtarɳakari ɔgɔ୍ni pɔri sukʰj୍mɔ |
in୍dɔ୍rij mɔnɔ ebɔŋ karɔɳɔ  emane kun୍tiŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ
eha paĩ luʈ eha sɔhit ehar naʈɔkɔre
eha mɔnus୍jɔku pagɔɭɔ kɔre taŋ୍ku pɔ୍rɔtarɳa kɔre |
teɳu tume b̤arɔtɔrɔ sɔ୍res୍ʈʰɔ sɔnɔ୍tan
tumɔrɔ hr̩dɔjɔku sasɔnɔ kɔrɔ bad̤ap୍rap୍tɔ ɔrɔ୍tʰɔ
mitʰ୍ja nɔrɔmɔ papku pɔ୍rɔtirୋd̤ɔ kɔrɔ d͡ʒaha
d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan ebɔŋ bit͡ʃarku nɔsɔ୍ʈɔ kɔre hɔ̃ sɔnsar sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi
kin୍tu d͡ʒaha ɔd̤ik sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi kɔre ebɔŋ mɔnɔ
sɔbuʈʰaru sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi ebɔŋ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sasɔkɔ pɔ୍raɳku ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ kɔrɔ |
ɔteb d͡ʒie sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ sasɔnɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti taŋ୍ku ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔri
nid͡ʒ pɔ୍raɳre at୍mar sɔmɔ୍pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ sɔkɔ୍ti bahar kɔrɔ
d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ sɔtɔ୍ru ebɔŋ sɔnɔ୍dehku pɔras୍tɔ kɔrɔ pɔ୍rij hirୋ hɔtɔ୍ja
kɔrɔ tumku b̤ɔlɔ akarre kɔɳɔ hɔnɔ୍tɔsɔnɔ୍tɔ kɔre ebɔŋ bis୍wasg̤atɔkɔta kɔrib

 ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun ebɔŋ tumɔrɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔru mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ

maja dɔ୍wara mɔୋrɔ d͡ʒadu dɔ୍wara d͡ʒaha mũ
b̤asman pɔ୍rɔkr̩tipʰɔrɔ୍mɔ upre muɭ bis୍tr̩t 
mũ ase ebɔŋ d͡ʒae ebɔŋ ase | d͡ʒetebeɭe d̤ar୍mikta
hɔ୍ras hue he b̤arɔtɔ d͡ʒetebeɭe dus୍ʈɔta

dr̩s୍jɔman rup d̤arɔɳɔ kɔre ebɔŋ purusɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔhit d͡ʒɔɳe bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍tiŋ୍ku
t͡ʃɔɭaibi b̤ɔlɔku sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ kɔre mɔnɔ୍dɔku pɔt͡ʃʰɔku ʈʰeli die

ebɔŋ mɔୋrɔ  sɔ୍wɔrij kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒetebeɭe se mansɔ t͡ʃʰaɖɔnɔ୍ti
tar b̤ar upre au rɔkʰɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ pr̩tʰibi d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔku au pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti nahĩ
 pɔ୍rij pɔ୍rin୍sɔ mɔୋ pakʰku asɔnɔ୍ti
seʈʰare ɔnek lɔୋkɔ asɔnɔ୍ti b̤ɔjɔru muk୍tɔ

mɔୋ sɔhit mɔୋrɔ mis୍rɔɳɔ | d͡ʒeũmane mɔୋte upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
mũ semanɔŋɔ୍ku un୍nɔtɔ kɔre kin୍tu sɔbuʈʰare sɔmɔsɔ୍te

kɔrɔ୍mɔ paĩ purɔsɔ୍kar kʰɔୋd͡ʒɔnɔ୍ti
bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman nim୍nɔ debtamanɔŋɔ୍ku bɔɭidan diɔnɔ୍ti | mũ tumku kɔhut͡ʃʰi
eʈʰare semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ purɔsɔ୍kar ɔt͡ʃʰi | kin୍tu mũ se
t͡ʃari d͡ʒati tiari kɔrit͡ʃʰi ebɔŋ
semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ guɳ ebɔŋ uphar pɔre semanɔŋɔ୍ku ek sɔ୍tʰan baɳ୍ʈit͡ʃʰi | hɔ̃ mũ
sr̩s୍ʈi ripୋd͡ʒɔpʰul୍ mũ
ɔmɔrɔ b̤abre bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃit͡ʃʰi sehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ sr̩s୍ʈi kɔrit͡ʃʰi kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ
paĩ maʈi mɔୋrɔ muɭ nuhẽ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔguɖ଼ik
ɔbib̤ɔkɔ୍tɔ hɔୋisarit͡ʃʰi | ebɔŋ teɳu ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔri sehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sad̤umane pɔrit୍raɳ paibaku t͡ʃes୍ʈa kɔle | tume d͡ʒepri kam kɔrɔ  ɔtitre tumɔrɔ pitr̩purusmane kɔritʰile।





apɔɳɔ kuhɔnɔ୍ti bib୍rɔtɔ eha pur୍bɔru gajɔkɔ ebɔŋ sad̤umanɔŋɔ୍kɔ dɔ୍  ara pɔt͡ʃɔrad͡ʒaitʰila  kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔɳɔ
ebɔŋ keũ nis୍kɔ୍rijta mũ apɔɳɔŋɔ୍ku eha sikʰaibi
ebɔŋ d͡ʒaɳi apɔɳɔ d͡ʒaɳibe keũ kam abɔsɔ୍jɔkɔtaku bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃaib
sehi tinid͡ʒɔɳɔŋɔ୍ku sɔʈʰik୍ b̤abre d̤ɔ୍jan kɔriba abɔsɔ୍jɔkɔ |

d͡ʒɔɭɔʈʰaru ɔd̤ik lɔʈapɔtɔ୍rɔ | ।
d͡ʒibɔnɔ sɔhit hr̩dɔjɔ sɔhit mɔnɔ sɔhit na
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ paɲ୍t͡ʃɔ in୍dɔ୍rijɔrɔ sahad͡ʒ୍jɔre  at୍mɔnir୍b̤ɔrɔsiɭ hebaku 
d͡ʒɔୋgimane semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ at୍ma ​​muk୍tɔ heba digre sɔrɔ୍bɔda pɔris୍rɔmɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti |
ehipri b̤ɔୋʈɔrɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ pʰɔɭɔ tɔ୍jag kɔri
ɔsim san୍ti lab̤ kɔrɔnɔ୍tu ɔbis୍wasi ut୍sahɔbɔnɔ୍d̤ɔnɔ
kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔru pʰɔɭɔ kʰɔୋd͡ʒiba bɔnɔ୍dɔ hɔୋid͡ʒae |
abis୍kr̩t  si taŋ୍kɔ at୍ma ​​mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jahar kɔri
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre nɔɔʈi geʈwe tʰiba sɔhɔrɔre  sɔ୍wɔrɔŋɔ୍kɔ pɔri bɔsitʰae
  #  na kit͡ʃʰi kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ kim୍ba kɔ
 ɳɔsi kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ | ehi d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u
kɔ  ɳɔsi kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ kim୍ba kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ pɔ୍rɔti ag୍rɔhɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ kim୍ba kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ
pʰɔɭɔ paĩ lɔୋb̤ɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ purusɔrɔ nid͡ʒɔsɔ୍wɔ
esbuku ʈʰelidie ehi d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ guru
nid͡ʒe kɔ  ɳɔsi mɔnus୍jɔrɔ b̤ɔlɔ ba mɔnɔ୍dɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
 bahare bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti manbikɔta eʈʰare
mur୍kʰɔta ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan dɔ୍wara | kin୍tu kaha paĩ |
at୍mar sehi ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar alୋkɔ dɔ୍wara gɔୋɖɔ଼aitʰae
t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar ebɔŋ sɔ୍wɔt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃʰɔ d͡ʒɔ୍jɔୋti sɔtɔ୍jɔku dɔrɔ୍sae
d͡ʒepri d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ ek sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ
ehar pɔ୍rɔb̤atɔrɔ alୋkɔku  aɭiba paĩ | se tɔtʰapi d̤ɔ୍jan kɔrutʰile
taŋ୍ku kʰɔୋd͡ʒutʰile taŋ୍kɔ sɔhit misitʰile taŋ୍kɔ upre rɔhile
alୋkit at୍mamane sehi ras୍taku
d͡ʒaan୍ti d͡ʒaha pɔt͡ʃʰɔku pʰeri nɔtʰae  semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ pap
bis୍wasɔrɔ sɔkɔ୍ti dɔ୍wara t͡ʃaligla | kie ehi alୋkɔ paib
d͡ʒie ehaku dekʰe। d͡ʒie bud୍d̤iman b̤abre dekʰe
bɔ୍rah୍mɔɳɔ nid͡ʒ pus୍tɔkɔ ebɔŋ pɔbit୍rɔta sɔhit
ga  hati ɔsut͡ʃi kukur
bahag̤ɔrɔ kukur mansɔrɔ mansɔ ek।
dunia pɔrad͡ʒit hɔୋit͡ʃʰi  are epriki eʈʰare
d͡ʒepri ekta upre semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ bis୍was sɔ୍tʰir kɔrɔnɔ୍tu |
paphin bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍ma ekta re bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
ebɔŋ semane bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍ma re bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti | ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik anɔnɔ୍dit huɔ nahĩ
 ebɔŋ ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik du  kʰi huɔ nahĩ du  kʰɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍mukʰin huɔ
 kin୍tu bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍ma upre rɔhila tɔtʰapi
kɔnɔsɔ୍ʈaɳ୍ʈɔ pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jekɔŋɔ୍ku rɔhibaku diɔ  si d͡ʒahar at୍ma
​​bah୍jɔ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kɔru durei d͡ʒae nid͡ʒ b̤itre
sukʰ pae d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ sɔhit bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maŋ୍ku d͡ʒɔୋgɔ kɔle
taŋ୍kɔrɔ at୍ma ​​ɔnɔnɔ୍tɔ san୍tir sɔ୍wad t͡ʃakʰe |
anɔnɔ୍dɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔru asitʰiba anɔnɔ୍dɔguɖ଼ik kin୍tu gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔku tɔ୍wɔran୍wit kɔre
d͡ʒaha nis୍t͡ʃit du  kʰɔ sr̩s୍ʈi kɔre sehi anɔnɔ୍dɔguɖ଼ik arɔmɔ୍b̤ɔ ebɔŋ ses hue
d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani mɔnɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi anɔnɔ୍dɔ pae nahĩ kun୍tiŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ
sehi pɔri kin୍tu d͡ʒɔdi d͡ʒɔɳe bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti sikʰib
se bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃitʰiba beɭe ebɔŋ nid͡ʒ sɔrirɔrɔ sr̩ŋ୍kʰɔɭa bɔhɔnɔ kɔre
lɔୋb̤ɔ ebɔŋ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔku ajɔtɔ୍tɔ kɔriba paĩ se ɔtɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ nin୍dɔnij
se heut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti jukʈa taŋ୍kɔ b̤itre sukʰ
sɔnɔ୍tus୍ʈɔta alୋkɔ ɔt͡ʃʰi taŋ୍kɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ
bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maŋ୍kɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔre mis୍rit hɔୋit͡ʃʰi se nir୍baɳ sɔ୍pɔrɔ୍sɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
ehipri  simane bis୍ram nebaku d͡ʒaan୍tu d͡ʒeũmane
pap dur hɔୋi bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti sɔnɔ୍dehre sesre hr̩dɔjɔre
sasit ebɔŋ san୍tɔ ruhɔnɔ୍ti | semane bas kɔrutʰiba sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ b̤ɔlɔre anɔnɔ୍dit
 sɔ୍bɔrɔŋɔ୍kɔ san୍ti nikɔʈɔre ebɔŋ sehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ
d͡ʒeũmane lɔୋb̤ɔ ebɔŋ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔru muk୍tɔ huɔnɔ୍ti
at୍mɔ ebɔŋ in୍dɔ୍rijmanɔŋɔ୍ku bɔsib̤ut kɔrɔnɔ୍ti at୍ma ​​d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti
sɔnɔ୍tʰɔ d͡ʒie nid͡ʒ pɔ୍lasiɖ୍ pɔ୍raɳ bahare bɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ɔrɔ୍tʰɔrɔ sɔ୍pɔrɔ୍sɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kɔku dei nɔtʰae |
d͡ʒahar san୍tɔ akʰi sɔ୍tʰir bɔ୍raud͡ʒru sid̤a dekʰe
d͡ʒahar bah୍jɔ nis୍was ebɔŋ b̤itɔrɔrɔ nis୍was
sɔman ebɔŋ nakru mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ d̤ir hɔୋid͡ʒae ebɔŋ bɔnɔ୍dɔ
sehi ek ɔŋɔ୍gɔ hr̩dɔjɔ ebɔŋ mɔnɔ bad̤it
muk୍ti upre nir୍b̤ɔrɔsiɭ
abeg b̤ɔjɔ ebɔŋ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔku durei rɔkʰit͡ʃʰi  bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman sud୍d̤a
muk୍ti pait͡ʃʰi sɔrɔ୍bɔda ebɔŋ sɔrɔ୍bɔda muk୍tɔ |
hɔ̃ karɔɳɔ se mɔୋte d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒie
bɔɭi o upasnaku d̤ɔ୍jan diɔnɔ୍ti  sɔ୍bɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔkas kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
ebɔŋ d͡ʒie d̤ɔ୍jan die nahĩ d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibit pɔ୍remi b̤ɔgɔban pɔ୍rɔkas kɔle
d͡ʒeũʈʰare kie surkʰja ebɔŋ  al paib
b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍ gita rɔ ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj eʈʰare ses hɔୋit͡ʃʰi
d͡ʒahar nam kɔrɔmasanasɔjɔୋgɔ
kim୍ba kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ pʰɔɭɔ tɔ୍jag kɔri d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ pus୍tɔkɔ।




ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
ɔteb d͡ʒie kam kɔribaku d͡ʒɔtʰar୍tʰɔ kɔre
kamru lab̤ kʰɔୋd͡ʒu nahĩ sehi bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti he pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
sanasi ebɔŋ d͡ʒɔୋgi  ub̤ɔjɔ gɔୋʈiere ɔt͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
ebɔŋ se nuhɔ̃nɔ୍ti d͡ʒie bɔɭir niã
d͡ʒaɭɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ kim୍ba kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre hat rɔkʰɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ |
pɔ୍rɔkr̩t tɔ୍jagkari b̤abre
kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍tu d͡ʒie kɔrɔ୍mɔ dɔ୍wara upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti karɔɳɔ d͡ʒie tɔ୍jag
kɔrɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒɔୋgin pɔri nuhẽ | sehipri b̤ɔlɔ b̤abre kuhad͡ʒait͡ʃʰi
kɔrɔ୍mɔ dɔ୍wara b̤ɔୋʈari bis୍  asku bɔ  e
ebɔŋ sad̤uta sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔru bɔnɔ୍dɔ hɔୋid͡ʒae
karɔɳɔ sɔmpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ d͡ʒɔୋgin kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti  kin୍tu
abeg dɔ୍  ara pɔ୍rɔb̤abit hɔୋintʰae ebɔŋ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ dɔ୍  ara simit hɔୋintʰae
pʰɔɭapʰɔɭɔku pr̩tʰɔkɔ kɔridie |
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti
at୍mɔ dɔ୍wara at୍mɔku bɔ  ଼aibaku diɔnɔ୍tu nid͡ʒ padku pɔdɔdɔɭit kɔrɔnɔ୍tu nahĩ
d͡ʒehetu at୍mar bɔnɔ୍d̤u heut͡ʃʰi at୍mɔrɔ sɔtɔ୍ru bɔ  ipare |
at୍mɔ at୍mɔrɔ bɔnɔ୍d̤u d͡ʒetebeɭe sel୍pʰɔ୍ nijɔmɔ kɔre
kin୍tu at୍mɔ sɔtɔ୍ru hɔୋid͡ʒae d͡ʒɔdi at୍mar at୍mɔ nid͡ʒku
g̤r̩ɳa kɔre |  # 

d͡ʒie at୍mɔnir୍b̤ɔrɔsiɭ ebɔŋ san୍tire d͡ʒibɔnɔ bitaut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti sehi sar୍bɔb̤ɔ  mɔ at୍ma
​​nid͡ʒ b̤itre ken୍dɔ୍rib̤ut sɔman
anɔnɔ୍dɔ ebɔŋ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔɳaku gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔre ut୍tap tʰɔɳɔ୍ɖa gɔ  rɔbɔ ebɔŋ lɔd͡ʒɔ୍d͡ʒa |
se d͡ʒɔୋgi se heut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti jukʈa
alୋkɔ ebɔŋ sɔtɔ୍jɔrɔ anɔnɔ୍dɔre anɔnɔ୍dit ɔlɔga
rɔhiba

 ehi t͡ʃih୍nɔ dɔ୍ 
ara se satʰi bɔnɔ୍d̤u
t͡ʃan୍sɔkɔmɔrɔ୍sɔ ɔpɔrit͡ʃit bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti pɔ୍remi sɔtɔ୍ru
elien୍ ebɔŋ sɔmɔ୍pɔrɔ୍kijmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ sɔman ɔnug୍rɔhɔrɔ d͡ʒɔɳasuɳa | sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku b̤ɔlɔ paiba
mɔnɔ୍dɔ kim୍ba b̤ɔlɔ |
se bɔsiba ut͡ʃit୍
sɔ୍tʰir b̤abre d̤ɔ୍jan kɔriba ekaki
taŋ୍kɔrɔ t͡ʃin୍tad̤ara nijɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rit taŋ୍kɔrɔ abeg dur hɔୋigla
d͡ʒinis t͡ʃʰaɖ | ek meɭare tɔtʰapi sɔ୍pɔʈɔ୍
taŋ୍kɔrɔ sɔ୍tʰir basɔsɔ୍tʰan ɔt͡ʃʰi  ɔd̤ik bɔ  ଼i nahĩ
kim୍ba epɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ kɔmɔ୍ nuhẽ  taŋ୍ku rɔhibaku diɔnɔ୍tu taŋ୍kɔ samɔgɔ୍ri
ek kɔpɔɖa hɔɭɔdia ebɔŋ kusag̤as |
seʈʰare taŋ୍kɔrɔ mɔnɔ upre kɔʈʰin sɔ୍tʰir kɔriba
hr̩dɔjɔ ebɔŋ in୍dɔ୍rijguɖ଼iku rɔୋkiba nirɔbɔ san୍tɔ
se d͡ʒɔୋgɔku sɔpʰɔɭɔ kɔrɔ ebɔŋ
at୍mar sud୍d̤ɔta hasɔlɔ kɔriba ɔsɔ୍tʰabɔrɔ
sɔrir ebɔŋ bek ebɔŋ muɳ୍ɖɔku d̤ɔri
taŋ୍kɔ nak sesre  # 



sehi d͡ʒɔୋgin ete nis୍ʈʰapɔrɔ ete nijɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rit
bahare san୍tire ase  mɔୋrɔ san୍ti
ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ nir୍baɳɔrɔ san୍ti
kin୍tu par୍tʰib abɔsɔ୍jɔkɔta paĩ
d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ taŋ୍kɔrɔ nuhẽ d͡ʒie ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik upbas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
kim୍ba ɔd̤ik b̤ɔୋd͡ʒi kɔrɔnɔ୍ti kim୍ba d͡ʒie
nirɔrɔ୍tʰɔkɔ mɔnɔru durei d͡ʒaan୍ti kim୍ba d͡ʒie sɔd͡ʒagtare
nid͡ʒɔrɔ sɔkɔ୍ti nɔsɔ୍ʈɔ kɔribaku pin୍d̤ɔnɔ୍ti | na ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun pɔ୍rɔkr̩t d̤ar୍mikta
d͡ʒaha
pr̩tʰibid͡ʒɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔɳa ebɔŋ ɔsus୍tʰɔtaku dur kɔritʰae d͡ʒeũʈʰare
kʰaiba ebɔŋ bis୍ram ebɔŋ kɔ୍riɖ଼are mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔmɔ ɔʈe
it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa ebɔŋ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre map kɔrad͡ʒae sɔୋiba beʈim
ɖɔ୍juʈi paĩ beʈim d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ |
d͡ʒetebeɭe sehi bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti
teɳu d͡ʒibit taŋ୍kɔ at୍maku ken୍dɔ୍rɔ kɔri t͡ʃin୍taku
sɔnd͡ʒɔmɔ b̤abre sɔnd͡ʒɔmɔ kɔla  ab୍̤jɔnɔ୍tɔriɳ b̤abre t͡ʃʰuĩla
b̤abna dɔ୍wara  tebe se heut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti jukʈa | dekʰɔnɔ୍tu
sɔ୍tʰir b̤abre pɔbɔnɔru as୍rɔjɔ paitʰiba ek pɔ୍rɔdip d͡ʒɔɭut͡ʃʰi
d͡ʒɔୋgiŋ୍kɔ mɔnɔrɔ sɔmanta heut͡ʃʰi in୍dɔ୍rij  ɖɔru
bɔnɔ୍dɔ hɔୋi sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔ pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ d͡ʒɔɭut͡ʃʰi |
d͡ʒetebeɭe mɔnɔ bɔ୍rɔୋɖɔ୍ pɔ୍lasiɖ୍ pɔbit୍rɔ ɔb̤ɔ୍jas sɔhit san୍tɔ hue
d͡ʒetebeɭe sel୍pʰɔ୍ at୍mɔ bisɔjɔre t͡ʃin୍ta kɔre ebɔŋ nid͡ʒe
hatʰ୍ san୍tɔ୍wɔna d͡ʒetebeɭe eha namhin anɔnɔ୍dɔ d͡ʒaɳe
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ɔrɔ୍tʰɔrɔ bahare pɔ୍raɳku pɔ୍rɔkasit 
kebɔɭɔ pɔ୍raɳ paĩ ebɔŋ d͡ʒaɳe dur hue nahĩ
ɔd̤ik sɔtɔ୍jɔku sɔtɔ kɔre d͡ʒetebeɭe ehaku d̤ɔri
eha ɔnɔ୍jɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi d̤ɔnɔku tuɭnat୍mɔkɔ mɔne kɔre nahĩ
kin୍tu seʈʰare rɔkʰad͡ʒaitʰiba ut୍ted͡ʒit kim୍ba kɔmɔ୍pit hɔୋiparib nahĩ |
d͡ʒek  ɳɔsi gɔb̤ir du  kʰɔ dɔ୍wara sehi rad͡ʒ୍jɔku san୍ti bɔୋli kuh
sehi kʰusir d͡ʒɔୋgɔ sehi bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍tiŋ୍ku
sid୍d̤ɔ d͡ʒɔୋgin bɔୋli ɖak
dr̩  b̤abre it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa etʰire
pɔris୍rɔmɔ kɔribaku pɔɖib d͡ʒepɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ pɔ୍rɔjas sɔhɔd͡ʒɔre ses nɔheba pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ
ebɔŋ t͡ʃin୍ta b̤abnaru t͡ʃaligla |
kʰɔ୍jati ebɔŋ lab̤ɔrɔ sɔ୍wɔpɔ୍nɔ dɔ୍wara ut୍pɔnɔ୍nɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ laɭsaku hɔlaiba 
in୍dɔ୍rijguɖikɔrɔ dɔ୍war bɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔriba
d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ war୍ɖɔ sɔhit teɳu pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jaj kɔ୍rɔme eha
san୍tir upharɔku ase ebɔŋ hr̩dɔjɔ as୍wasit hue
d͡ʒetebeɭe mɔnɔ at୍mabr̩t hɔୋi rɔhe ebɔŋ at୍ma ​​kam୍bɔrɔ୍les୍ bɔ୍rɔୋɖɔ୍ kɔre
| kin୍tu d͡ʒetetʰɔrɔ hr̩dɔjɔ
b̤aŋ୍gid͡ʒae  d͡ʒɔŋɔ୍gɔli ebɔŋ hɔlɔt͡ʃɔlɔ  nijɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔɳɔru teɳu
taŋ୍ku barɔmɔ୍bar ehaku bɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔribaku diɔnɔ୍tu se ehaku punɔrɔ୍bar
pɔ୍raɳɔrɔ sasɔnɔku pʰerai diɔnɔ୍tu | sid୍d̤ɔ sukʰ paĩ
kebɔɭɔ kɔୋɭɔre san୍tɔ hue
at୍ma ​​ut୍sahhin ɔpɔrad̤ru sud୍d̤ɔ
ɔsim pɔ୍rɔtid͡ʒ୍ɲa | d͡ʒie ehipri sɔpɔtʰɔ kɔre
sɔrɔ୍bɔୋpɔri at୍maku taŋ୍kɔrɔ at୍ma pap t͡ʃʰaɖi bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maŋ୍kɔ sɔhit ektar
ɔsim sukʰre bad̤a sr̩s୍ʈi kɔre |
se ete sɔpɔtʰɔ kɔle
ete mis୍rit d͡ʒibɔnɔpɔ୍raɳ basin୍da
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibre ebɔŋ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibɔd͡ʒɔnɔ୍tu
sehi d͡ʒibɔnɔpɔ୍raɳre dekʰɔnɔ୍ti | ebɔŋ
d͡ʒie mɔୋte ebɔŋ mɔୋ b̤itre sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku t͡ʃih୍nitʰae
mũ taŋ୍ku kebebi d͡ʒibaku debi nahĩ se
mɔୋte d̤ɔri rɔkʰɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ। kin୍tu se d͡ʒeũʈʰare rɔhibe
taŋ୍kɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ kɔɳɔ mɔୋ b̤itre se bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔnɔ୍ti
karɔɳɔ se mɔୋte d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti o upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒie
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔre bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ mɔୋ sɔhit d͡ʒɔɖit ɔʈɔnɔ୍ti |
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun d͡ʒɔdi d͡ʒɔɳe bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti sɔbuaɖe dekʰe
 nid͡ʒɔrɔ sɔmanta dɔ୍wara sikʰja diad͡ʒae  gɔୋʈie d͡ʒibɔnɔ
​​mɔnɔ୍dɔ ebɔŋ b̤ɔlɔre
gɔୋʈie mɔhɔtɔ୍tɔ୍  taŋ୍ku ek d͡ʒɔୋgi d̤ɔri rɔkʰɔ hɔ̃ b̤ɔlɔsɔmpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
mɔd̤uŋ୍kɔ hɔtɔ୍jakari tɔtʰapi punɔrɔ୍bar ehi d͡ʒɔୋgɔ
ehi san୍ti sɔmantaru ut୍pɔnɔ୍nɔ
tum dɔ୍wara d͡ʒɔɳasuɳa  mũ etʰire kɔ  ɳɔsi sɔ୍tʰirta dekʰu nahĩ
 bis୍ram nahĩ karɔɳɔ mɔnus୍jɔrɔ hr̩dɔjɔ
ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij kr̩s୍ɳɔ rag ɔsan୍tɔ
it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰasɔkɔ୍tɔ ebɔŋ sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi | mũ b̤abut͡ʃʰi
mɔnus୍jɔrɔ hr̩dɔjɔ pɔri pɔtʰɔhin pɔbɔnɔku d̤ɔri rɔkʰiba |
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
hirୋ dir୍g̤ɔsɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ ɔsɔ୍wikar kɔriba bahare kɔʈʰin
mɔnus୍jɔrɔ hr̩dɔjɔ heut͡ʃʰi sɔnd͡ʒɔmɔta ebɔŋ hɔlɔt͡ʃɔlɔ
tɔtʰapi eha ɔb̤ɔ୍jas dɔ୍wara pɔ୍rɔtibɔnɔ୍d̤it hɔୋipare pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
sɔ୍wɔkɔmaɳ୍ɖɔ୍ dɔ୍wara | ehi d͡ʒɔୋgɔ mũ kɔhut͡ʃʰi
ɔɳɔsɔnrɔkʰjit lɔୋkɔŋɔ୍ku haluka b̤abe ase nahĩ
kin୍tu d͡ʒie nid͡ʒku guru kɔrib
 se d͡ʒitib d͡ʒɔdi se dr̩  b̤abre t͡ʃes୍ʈa kɔre |
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
ebɔŋ d͡ʒie bis୍was kɔre
bipʰɔɭɔ hue kr̩s୍ɳɔ pɔ୍rɔjasre
pɔbit୍rɔtaʈʰaru pʰerid͡ʒiba  sɔmpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ nijɔmɔ hɔraiba
se hɔd͡ʒi nahãnɔ୍ti bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maŋ୍kɔ alୋkɔru bit͡ʃ୍jut
ɔsar meg̤ pɔri d͡ʒaha pr̩tʰibi ebɔŋ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔre b̤asut͡ʃʰi
d͡ʒetebeɭe bid͡ʒuɭi ehaku duib̤ag kɔre ebɔŋ eha ɔdr̩s୍jɔ hue
du  kʰɔ mũ tumku eʈʰare ut୍tɔrɔ debar suɳibi
d͡ʒehetu kr̩s୍ɳɔ tume kebɔɭɔ sɔnɔ୍deh dur kɔriparib nahĩ |
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
se hɔd͡ʒi nahãnɔ୍ti he pɔ୍ritar put୍rɔ na
na pr̩tʰibi na sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ taŋ୍kɔ paĩ bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃit
karɔɳɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi hr̩dɔjɔ d͡ʒie gɔୋʈie sɔʈʰik୍ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa d̤arɔɳɔ kɔre
 se kʰjɔtir ras୍taku gɔti kɔre nahĩ d͡ʒie d̤ar୍mik heba paĩ bipʰɔɭɔ hue se
mr̩t୍ju sɔmɔjɔre d̤ar୍mik
ɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔɭɔku ase seʈʰare
maphin bɔrɔ୍sɔ bas kɔre ebɔŋ punɔrɔ୍bar d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ hɔୋi  saman୍jɔ ebɔŋ kʰusi mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre
punɔrɔ୍bar kit͡ʃʰi sun୍dɔrɔ g̤ɔre d͡ʒibɔnɔ arɔmɔ୍b̤ɔ kɔre |
eha
sɔmɔ୍b̤ɔbɔtɔ  se guɳɔrɔ sɔ୍tɔnɔ upre ek d͡ʒɔୋgin g̤ɔrɔku oh୍laibe
 kin୍tu eha birɔɭɔ ehipri d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ
ehi pr̩tʰibire paiba kɔsɔ୍ʈɔkɔrɔ mukʰ
teɳu se punɔrɔ୍bar hr̩dɔjɔrɔ keũ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔta
hasɔlɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ se punɔrɔ୍bar
sid୍d̤ɔta paĩ t͡ʃes୍ʈa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti b̤ɔlɔ asa sɔhit pɔ୍rij pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
karɔɳɔ puratɔnɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa dɔ୍wara se
ɔd͡ʒaɳɔtɔre akɔrɔ୍sit hue ebɔŋ kebɔɭɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa kɔriba
heut͡ʃʰi d͡ʒɔୋgɔrɔ sud୍d̤ɔta heut͡ʃʰi
sabɔdɔ୍rɔbɔmɔ୍ kɔtʰit bed ɔtik୍rɔmɔ kɔriba |
kin୍tu d͡ʒɔୋgi hɔୋi dr̩  ebɔŋ dir୍g̤ɔ pɔ୍rɔjas

pɔre se sesre
durre pad lɔgaile | d͡ʒepriki d͡ʒɔɳe
ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔkɔୋʈir upre d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanimanɔŋɔ୍kɔʈʰaru ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ
bis୍tr̩t kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ sɔpʰɔɭɔta bahare
tume d͡ʒɔୋgi ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun huɔ  ebɔŋ ehipri bis୍ 
as mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru sɔtɔ୍jɔ ebɔŋ sɔrɔ୍bɔୋtɔ୍tɔmɔ d͡ʒie mɔୋte ɔnɔ୍tɔrɔŋɔ୍gɔ
at୍ma ​​sɔhit upasna kɔre se mɔୋrɔ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔre rɔhila
eʈʰare ses ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj । b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍ gita
d͡ʒahar nam ɔʈɔmasanajୋgɔ

kr̩s୍ɳɔ
pɔ୍rij pɔ୍rin୍sɔ kipri d͡ʒɔdi tumɔrɔ pɔ୍raɳ
mɔୋ upre sɔrɔ୍bɔda sɔ୍tʰapit hue  tɔtʰapi d͡ʒɔୋgɔku bɔ୍jajam kɔre
tɔtʰapi mɔୋte tumɔrɔ sɔrɔɳar୍tʰi kɔrɔ  tume
nis୍t͡ʃit b̤abre mɔୋ pakʰku asib |

d͡ʒaɳib ehi duniare au d͡ʒaɳibaku t͡ʃʰaɖib nahĩ |
ɔnek hɔd͡ʒare mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru gɔୋʈie
pɔrɔ୍t͡ʃan୍sɔ sɔtɔ୍jɔ paĩ t͡ʃes୍ʈa ebɔŋ sehi ɔɭɔ୍pɔ lɔୋkɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ
mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru  na ebɔŋ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔku uʈʰ  kebɔɭɔ d͡ʒɔɳe  eʈʰare ebɔŋ seʈʰare 
mɔୋte d͡ʒaɳe mũ d͡ʒepri sɔtɔ୍jɔ ɔʈe |
pr̩tʰibi d͡ʒɔɭɔ ɔgɔ୍ni baju itʰɔrɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ ​​ebɔŋ mɔnɔ
ebɔŋ bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍tigɔtɔta  sehi aʈʰʈi
mɔୋrɔ mɔnipʰes୍ʈɔ୍ pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ kɔre |
eguɖ଼ik mɔୋrɔ nim୍nɔ pɔ୍rɔkr̩ti ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔku sikʰ d͡ʒeũtʰire
 tume sahsi ehi bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔ
 d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ niti ɔnud͡ʒaji ut୍padit hue
d͡ʒeũtʰire dr̩s୍jɔman d͡ʒinisguɖ଼ikɔrɔ sɔnsar
ek jɔୋni pɔri d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ hue | d͡ʒaɳ mũ sehi gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔ
mũ ehi bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔ tiari kɔre ebɔŋ tiari kɔre
mɔୋ ɔpekʰja ɔnɔ୍jɔ guru pɔ୍rin୍sɔ nahĩ
ɔnɔ୍jɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi nir୍mata nahĩ esbu mɔୋ upre

dus୍kɔrɔ୍mɔkari kim୍ba mur୍kʰɔ lɔୋkɔmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ d͡ʒɔɳa nahĩ
kim୍ba muɭ ebɔŋ t͡ʃurlis୍ kim୍ba d͡ʒeũmanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ

kim୍ba d͡ʒeũmane ɔsurasɔrɔ ras୍ta ɔbɔlɔmɔ୍bɔnɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti |  # 
t͡ʃari pɔ୍rɔkarɔrɔ mɔɳis mɔୋte d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒie kan୍dɔnɔ୍ti

ebɔŋ d͡ʒie sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ kɔribaku pɔris୍rɔmɔ kɔre ebɔŋ d͡ʒie mɔୋ upre bɔsitʰae
 se d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanban |
he t͡ʃarid͡ʒɔɳɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru

sehimane mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ ɔt͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒahar d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan
ehi it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa kim୍ba taha dɔ୍  ara semanɔŋɔ୍ku
ketek nim୍nɔ debtaŋ୍ku seba kɔribaku deitʰae bib̤in୍nɔ ritiniti sɔhit d͡ʒaha semanɔŋɔ୍ku pɔ୍rɔb̤abit kɔre | ehipri sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ  semane keũ mɔnɔ୍dir pud͡ʒa kɔribe keũ akr̩ti bis୍

bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mũ tum paĩ kʰɔୋlibi  d͡ʒahar hr̩dɔjɔ pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jakʰ୍jan kɔre
nahĩ  ses lɔୋrɔ gɔb̤irluk୍kajit
mɔୋrɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔ ebɔŋ pr̩tʰibir sehi durɔtɔmɔ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔ
d͡ʒaha d͡ʒaɳiba tumku ɔsus୍tʰɔtaru muk୍tɔ kɔrib 
ek rad͡ʒkij lɔୋrɔ ek rad͡ʒa rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔ
hɔ̃ pɔ୍ret୍jɔkɔkɔ
papru muk୍ti paib। pɔbit୍rɔtar alୋkɔ ɔti
t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar mɔhima sɔhit dekʰibaku sɔrɔɭɔ
t͡ʃaliba sɔhɔd͡ʒɔ ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij
d͡ʒeũmane eha gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ bis୍  asre bipʰɔɭɔ huɔnɔ୍ti
ɔd̤ik d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan bu  iba paĩ mɔୋ
sɔtɔ୍rumanɔŋɔ୍kɔ binaskari mɔୋ pakʰre pɔhɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔnɔ୍tu nahĩ semane punɔrɔ୍bar
buɖ଼igle d͡ʒeũʈʰare sɔbu d͡ʒinis bɔdɔɭid͡ʒae
mɔୋ dɔ୍  ara d͡ʒinisguɖ଼ikɔrɔ sɔmɔgɔ୍rɔ bisaɭ bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔ
bis୍tar hɔୋit͡ʃʰi  mɔୋ dɔ୍  ara ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲat
mɔୋ b̤itre sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ɔsɔ୍tit୍wɔ ɔt͡ʃʰi
mũ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ b̤itre nuhẽ
tɔtʰapi seguɖ଼ik d̤arɔɳɔ kɔre nahĩ
sehi dr̩s୍jɔman d͡ʒinisguɖik
rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔku gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔribaku t͡ʃes୍ʈa kɔrɔ  mɔୋrɔ
sr̩s୍ʈi  sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku sr̩s୍ʈi kɔriba sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃaiba  tɔtʰapi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍kɔ
bahare bas kɔre
dekʰɔnɔ୍tu d͡ʒehetu kuɭhin baju
maphin d͡ʒagare gɔti kɔre kin୍tu sɔ୍tʰan nuhẽ
ebɔŋ t͡ʃɔɭɔpɔ୍rɔt͡ʃɔɭɔ baju bina sɔ୍tʰan tʰila
teɳu sɔbu d͡ʒinis mɔୋ b̤itre ɔt͡ʃʰi kin୍tu mũ nuhẽ |
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek kalpa bɔnɔ୍dɔ heba sɔmɔjɔre b̤artij pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒinis d͡ʒaha mɔୋ sr̩s୍ʈiku pʰeri ase
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek kɔlɔpa arɔmɔ୍b̤ɔre
mɔୋ ʈʰaru nutɔnɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mit sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ bisɔjɔ |
sɔkɔ୍ti
ebɔŋ pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir sahad͡ʒ୍jɔre mɔୋrɔ bah୍jɔ sel୍pʰɔ
punɔrɔ୍bar ebɔŋ tɔtʰapi mũ
dr̩s୍jɔman d͡ʒinisguɖikɔrɔ kʰjet୍rɔ  semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa bina 
sɔmɔsɔ୍te  pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir sɔkɔ୍ti dɔ୍wara |
tɔtʰapi ehi mɔhan nir୍maɳ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ mɔୋte d͡ʒɔɖit kɔrɔ
nahĩ mũ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔʈʰaru ɔlɔga
ɔnɔ୍jɔ ebɔŋ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ ebɔŋ muk୍tɔ bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman sɔnlɔgɔ୍nɔ hɔୋit͡ʃʰi
ehipri d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ d͡ʒinisguɖ଼ik mɔୋ dɔ୍wara gɔ
଼a d͡ʒaitʰae d͡ʒahaki gɔtisiɭ tɔtʰapi
d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ kim୍ba d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ ehipri d͡ʒɔgɔtɔ t͡ʃalib
mɔnɔ mɔୋte b̤ul୍ b̤ul୍ kɔla rupre at͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰadit
hela

br̩tʰa asa ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔriba br̩tʰa kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔriba
br̩tʰa d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanre kʰaibaku  ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲan b̤abre semane
ek mɔnɔ୍dɔ mar୍gɔ nis୍ʈʰur ebɔŋ b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ mar୍gɔ kʰɔୋd͡ʒɔnɔ୍ti |
kin୍tu mɔୋrɔ mɔhat୍magan୍d̤i d͡ʒeũmane
sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij pɔtʰɔre gɔti kɔrɔnɔ୍ti semane mɔୋte
hr̩dɔjɔ sɔhit upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti 
d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ ut୍sɔ tumɔrɔ ɔnɔnɔ୍tɔ ut୍sɔ mɔୋte d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti |
semane mɔୋte gɔ  rɔban୍wit kɔrɔnɔ୍ti। mɔୋte kʰɔୋd͡ʒɔ
mɔୋrɔ sɔmɔ୍man ebɔŋ pɔ୍remɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔtid͡ʒ୍ɲa paɭɔnɔ kɔrɔ pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔsiɭ bis୍was sɔhit mɔୋte adɔrɔ
kɔrɔ | hɔ̃ ebɔŋ d͡ʒeũmane mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
d͡ʒie d͡ʒag୍rɔtɔ hr̩dɔjɔrɔ bɔɭi ut୍sɔrɔ୍gɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
at୍maŋ୍kɔrɔ ek t͡ʃapku bu  ae
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek sɔ୍tʰanre gɔୋʈie pʰɔୋrɔ୍sɔ d͡ʒɔdio bɔhuguɳ
mũ bɔɭidan mũ pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna
mũ mr̩tmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ  eŋ୍kanaɭkek୍ seʈ୍
mũ arୋgɔ୍jɔkari  sɔd̤ɔ mũ g̤i
mɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ ebɔŋ niã ebɔŋ d͡ʒaha d͡ʒɔɭid͡ʒae
mũ ehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ simahin bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔrɔ
pita mata pitr̩purus ebɔŋ rakʰji
sikʰjar ses d͡ʒaha
lɔsɔ୍ʈɔ୍ral୍ paɳire sud୍d̤ɔ kɔre mũ  mũ
rig୍bed samabed jɔd͡ʒurbed
mar୍gɔ paɭɔkɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u bit͡ʃarɔpɔti
sakʰji basɔsɔ୍tʰan sɔrɔɳar୍tʰi gr̩h
bɔnɔ୍d̤u  rɔɳa ebɔŋ d͡ʒibɔnɔ sɔmud୍rɔ
d͡ʒaha pɔʈʰae ebɔŋ giɭitʰae duniar
b̤ɔɳɔ୍ɖar ebɔŋ b̤ɔɳɔ୍ɖart͡ʃam୍bɔrɔ bihɔnɔ ebɔŋ bihɔnɔ buɳa
ɔsim ɔmɔɭɔ keũʈʰaru ase sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ ut୍tap mɔୋrɔ
ɔnumti deba kim୍ba ɔʈɔkaiba paĩ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔrɔ bɔrɔ୍sa mɔୋrɔ
mr̩t୍ju mũ ebɔŋ ɔmɔrɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ mũ
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun  ebɔŋ  dr̩s୍jɔman d͡ʒibɔnɔ
​​ebɔŋ d͡ʒibɔnɔ ɔdr̩s୍jɔ
hɔ̃ d͡ʒeũmane
tiniguɳ bed sikʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒeũmane sɔୋmamɔdɔ piut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
pap sud୍d̤ɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti bɔɭi diɔnɔ୍ti  mɔୋ ʈʰaru semane sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔku
pas୍ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒeũʈʰare mansɔ  sɔ୍wɔrij ɔʈe |
mɔhan debtamanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru semanɔŋɔ୍ku ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ in୍dɔ୍rɔŋɔ୍kɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔre kʰaibaku diɔnɔ୍ti |
tɔtʰapi d͡ʒetebeɭe sehi sɔmɔ୍manɔd͡ʒɔnɔkɔ anɔnɔ୍dɔ ɔd̤ik
paradip kʰɔrɔ୍t͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ hue ebɔŋ diad͡ʒaitʰiba d͡ʒɔୋgɔ୍jɔta paĩ mɔd͡ʒuri
hue mr̩t୍ju d͡ʒɔgɔtɔku as ebɔŋ puɳi tʰɔre pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔ kɔrɔ |
semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ purɔsɔ୍kar tʰila
tiniguɳ sas୍tɔ୍rɔ ebɔŋ ehar lekʰa ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔri semane semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d̤ɔnɔ sɔnrɔkʰjɔɳɔ kɔle 
d͡ʒie eb̤ɭi ɔnɔ୍wesɔɳɔ kɔre se
asutʰiba anɔnɔ୍dɔku t͡ʃirɔsɔ୍tʰaji anɔnɔ୍dɔ pae | mũ semanɔŋɔ୍ku ɔnumti die
kin୍tu sehi asir୍bad pɔ୍rap୍tɔ bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍timanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ d͡ʒeũmane mɔୋte upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti ɔnɔ୍jɔ sɔ୍tʰanku
nɔ bulɔnɔ୍ti mɔnɔ sɔ୍tʰir hɔୋi
mũ pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ sukʰɔrɔ nis୍t͡ʃitta aɳitʰae |
na ebɔŋ hr̩dɔjɔ d͡ʒaha ɔnɔ୍jɔ debtaŋ୍ku ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ
kɔre sɔrɔɭɔ bis୍wasre semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna mɔୋ pakʰku ase
he kun୍ti put୍rɔ d͡ʒɔdio semane b̤ul୍ pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
karɔɳɔ mũ
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek bɔɭir pɔ୍rap୍tɔkɔrɔ୍tɔ୍ta ebɔŋ pɔ୍rɔb̤u d͡ʒaha emane ʈʰik୍ b̤abre d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ
 teɳu semane punɔrɔ୍bar pr̩tʰibiku pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti
d͡ʒeũmane debtamanɔŋɔ୍ku ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ debtamanɔŋɔ୍kɔ nikɔʈɔku d͡ʒaan୍ti
d͡ʒeũmane semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ at୍maku piʈ୍ris୍ pɔ୍rɔti sɔpɔtʰɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti mɔnɔ
dus୍ʈɔ b̤uʈmanɔŋɔ୍ku b̤uʈku buɖ଼ai diagla
d͡ʒie mɔୋte pɔ୍rem kɔre se mɔୋ pakʰku ase।
d͡ʒie mɔୋte bis୍was o pɔ୍remre ut୍sɔrɔ୍gɔ kɔrib
 gɔୋʈie pɔtɔ୍rɔ pʰul pʰɔɭɔ paɳi  aɭi diad͡ʒae
sehi uphar mũ gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔre sɔ୍nehpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ b̤abre
d̤ar୍mik it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰare tiari | pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
kʰaiba kim୍ba bɔɭidan uphar deba
pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kim୍ba upbas eha
mɔୋ paĩ heu mɔୋrɔ b̤ɔɭi | teɳu tume
kɔrɔmɔbɔnɔ୍d̤ɔru nid͡ʒku muk୍tɔ kɔrib sr̩ŋ୍kʰɔɭa d͡ʒaha mɔnus୍jɔku
b̤ɔlɔ ebɔŋ mɔnɔ୍dɔ pɔ୍rɔsɔŋɔ୍gɔre rɔkʰib teɳu
tume mɔୋ pakʰku nirapɔdɔre asib d͡ʒetebeɭe tume mansɔ t͡ʃʰaɖib  bis୍was ebɔŋ ɔpɔhɔrɔɳɔ
dɔ୍wara mɔୋ sɔhit d͡ʒɔୋgɔdan heb
mũ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ sɔman mũ d͡ʒaɳe g̤r̩ɳa kɔre nahĩ
mũ ɔnug୍rɔhɔ d͡ʒaɳe nahĩ d͡ʒaha tiari hɔୋit͡ʃʰi mɔୋrɔ
kin୍tu d͡ʒeũmane mɔୋte pɔ୍rem sɔhit upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti mũ semanɔŋɔ୍ku b̤ɔlɔ pae
semane mɔୋʈʰare ɔt͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ mũ semanɔŋɔ୍kɔʈʰare ɔt͡ʃʰi
na pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
d͡ʒɔdi kɔ  ɳɔsi mɔnɔ୍dɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ tar t͡ʃin୍tad̤arare
mɔୋ pakʰku d͡ʒae b̤ɔlɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre taŋ୍ku gɔɳɔna kɔrɔ
se ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ pɔtʰɔ bat͡ʃʰit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti se
dir୍g̤ɔ din d̤ɔri d̤ar୍mik hebe। se sehi san୍ti paibe
d͡ʒaha pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔ hue nahĩ | he b̤arɔtɔrɔ rad͡ʒkumar
nis୍t͡ʃit huɔ d͡ʒe kehi bi binɔsɔ୍ʈɔ hɔୋiparibe nahĩ mɔୋte bis୍was kɔri
he pɔ୍ritʰaŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ d͡ʒie mɔୋ pakʰku pʰerib d͡ʒɔdio semane pap sɔ୍tɔ୍ri kim୍ba purusɔrɔ
gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔru d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ hɔୋitʰile 
bɔ  sɔ୍ɳɔbɔ d͡ʒatir ut୍pɔtɔ୍ti
kim୍ba sud୍raŋ୍ku ɔbɔheɭa 
sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ ras୍tare sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ud୍b̤id pad tebe kipri
pɔbit୍rɔ bɔ୍rah୍mɔɳɔ ebɔŋ mɔୋrɔ rɔjal୍ sad̤umane
a  tume ehi ɔsus୍tʰɔ duniaku asit͡ʃʰ  pɔɭajɔnɔkari
ebɔŋ mitʰ୍ja  mɔୋ upre tumɔrɔ bis୍was sɔ୍tʰir kɔrɔ
hr̩dɔjɔ sɔ୍tʰir kɔrɔ ebɔŋ mɔୋ upre t͡ʃin୍ta kɔrɔ mɔୋte adɔrɔ kɔrɔ aɳ |
mɔୋte ɔpʰɔrɔ୍ mɔୋte pɔ୍rɔɳam kɔrɔ
mɔୋte tumɔrɔ sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ anɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔrɔ  ebɔŋ ɔbib̤ɔkɔ୍tɔ
mɔୋrɔ bis୍ram pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ tumɔrɔ at୍ma ​​mar୍gɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ kɔribe |
eʈʰare  ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ses hue | b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍ gita
akʰ୍ja bisis୍ʈɔ rad͡ʒabid୍  rɔd͡ʒaguhujୋgɔ
kim୍ba kiŋ୍gɔ୍ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan ebɔŋ kiŋ୍gɔ୍ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔ dɔ୍wara d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ pus୍tɔkɔ
।




ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj
kr̩s୍ɳɔ।  # 
au ɔd̤ik suɳ he dir୍g̤ɔ sɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u ehi nutɔnɔ sɔbɔ୍dɔguɖ଼ik mũ kɔhut͡ʃʰi
 tumku sukʰ ebɔŋ san୍ti aɳibaku kɔhili d͡ʒie mɔୋte sɔrɔ୍bɔda pɔ୍rem
kɔre   sɔ୍wɔrɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔhan kɔmɔ୍pani kim୍ba rad͡ʒa  si
mɔୋrɔ pɔ୍rɔkr̩ti d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti nahĩ d͡ʒie debta ebɔŋ  siŋ୍ku bɔhu pur୍bɔru sr̩s୍ʈi kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
se kebɔɭɔ d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍tikebɔɭɔ se papru muk୍tɔ ebɔŋ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani
d͡ʒie mɔୋte dekʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u bis୍wasalୋkit akʰire
d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mit ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij ɔbib̤ɔkɔ୍tɔ |
mɔɳis d͡ʒaha bitɔrɔɳɔ hue sehi pɔ୍rɔkr̩tiguɖ଼ik mɔୋʈʰaru ut୍pɔnɔ୍nɔ hue bud୍d̤i kɔ  sɔɭɔ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan d̤ɔ  rɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ

ebɔŋ sɔmɔ୍man ebɔŋ mɔd̤ur nirɔrɔ୍tʰɔkɔta  #  ebɔŋ san୍ti d͡ʒaha
sɔman

debaku it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa ebɔŋ sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ kɔribaku it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa  sɔmɔsɔ୍te ase | mɔୋrɔ uphar
satɔd͡ʒɔɳɔ mukʰ୍jɔ sad̤u pɔ୍rat͡ʃin t͡ʃari pɔ୍rɔb̤u manɔsɔ seʈ୍
 mɔୋrɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ baɳ୍ʈiba  d͡ʒɔgɔtɔku sasɔnɔ kɔriba paĩ mũ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ kɔli
ebɔŋ  sis୍ piʈ୍ris୍ manus୍ sɔmɔsɔ୍te mɔୋ mɔnɔrɔ gɔୋʈie t͡ʃin୍ta dɔ୍wara

hɔ̃ mɔୋte sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ ut୍sɔ d͡ʒaɳe mɔୋ dɔ୍  ara sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ pɔ୍raɳi sr̩s୍ʈi kɔle

mũ tumku mɔୋrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sɔmanta ɔsim d̤ɔni  sɔ୍wɔrij
mɔୋrɔ pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔsiɭ rɔŋɔ୍gɔ mɔୋrɔ ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ rup dekʰae | dekʰɔnɔ୍tu mɔୋrɔ ehi muhɔ̃re
adit୍jɔ b̤as୍ rud୍rɔ aswin୍sɔ ebɔŋ maruʈ୍sɔ sɔŋkʰɔ୍ja

dekʰ eha heut͡ʃʰi bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔ  dekʰ d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ ebɔŋ mr̩t kɔɳɔ
mũ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku ekaʈʰi kɔre  mɔୋ b̤itre dekʰ d͡ʒepri tumɔrɔ oʈʰ kɔhit͡ʃʰi
b̤ɔgɔban ɔnɔnɔ୍tɔkaɭre ɔti b̤ɔgɔban mɔୋte dekʰ tume kɔɳɔ pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kɔrut͡ʃʰ dekʰ
tume parib nahĩ  kim୍ba manɔbɔ akʰire ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun sɔrɔ୍bɔda majes୍ʈɔ
teɳu mũ tumku  sɔ୍wɔrij ɔnub̤ɔbɔ kɔre | ɔnɔ୍jɔ akʰi nua alୋkɔ
ebɔŋ dekʰ eha mɔୋrɔ gɔ  rɔbɔ mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔ dr̩s୍jɔ paĩ un୍mɔୋt͡ʃit
sɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔjɔ |
he mɔharad͡ʒ b̤ɔgɔban teɳu kɔhitʰle
pɔ୍ritaŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔŋɔ୍ku taŋ୍kɔrɔ bisaɭ sɔrɔ୍bɔsɔkɔ୍timanɔrɔ
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ mɔhima as୍t͡ʃɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ b̤ɔjɔ dekʰaile | ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ akʰiru ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ paʈiru ades deutʰiba ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔmɔjɔ pʰɔrɔ୍mɔguɖik ek rupre pɔripur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik ʈʰia hɔୋitʰiba ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ gɔ  rɔbɔ ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij ɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ d̤arɔɳɔ sɔ୍ʈarɔkɔ୍lɔsɔ୍ʈɔrɔ gar୍lɔpʰɔ୍reɳ୍ɖɔre mukuʈ pin୍d̤itʰiba buɳad͡ʒaitʰiba lus୍ʈɔrɔ pɔୋsakre pɔrihit taŋ୍kɔʈʰaru nis୍was neba | sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij gɔnɔ୍d̤ɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek sukʰj୍mɔ mɔhɔtɔ୍tɔ୍  rɔ upd͡ʒuk୍tɔ upɔsɔ୍tʰiti  dr̩s୍ʈihin ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔta  aɭiba  ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik bis୍tar  simahin sun୍dɔrɔ  sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sɔ୍pes୍ |














taŋ୍kɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ mukʰ sɔhit
teɳu se dekʰaile d͡ʒɔdi
hɔʈʰat୍ akas mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre uʈʰiba ut͡ʃit
 ek hɔd͡ʒar sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ
kirɔɳɔ pr̩tʰibiku ɔbib̤ɔkɔ୍tɔ bim୍ sɔhit bɔnɔ୍ja pɔris୍tʰiti sr̩s୍ʈi kɔre
tebe huet sehi pɔbit୍rɔ bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍tiŋ୍kɔ
mɔhima ebɔŋ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔta sɔ୍wɔpɔ୍nɔre dekʰipare
paɳ୍ɖuŋ୍kɔ put୍rɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔ dekʰile d͡ʒe
ehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔ
ehar sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ biraʈ bibid̤taku
ek bisaɭ akarre pɔriɳɔtɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰi ebɔŋ
dr̩s୍jɔman heb ebɔŋ dekʰad͡ʒib ebɔŋ
ek sɔrirre mis୍rit heb  sukʰj୍mɔ t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar
namhin  sɔrɔ୍bɔbu
 utʰiba b̤ɔgɔban b̤ɔgɔban kɔdapi nuhẽ |  debta ses

kin୍tu ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik as୍t͡ʃɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ
rɔୋmaɲ୍t͡ʃit pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kr̩t ebɔŋ t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kr̩t
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun aɳ୍ʈʰumaɖi se muɳ୍ɖɔ nuãi
papuli d̤ɔritʰile। se t͡ʃit୍kar kɔri kɔhila
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
hɔ̃ mũ dekʰi sarit͡ʃʰi mũ dekʰut͡ʃʰi
pɔ୍rɔb̤u sɔmɔsɔ୍te tum b̤itre abr̩t
debtamane tumɔrɔ gɔ  rɔbɔmɔjɔ pʰɔ୍remre ɔt͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
pr̩tʰibi sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔ ebɔŋ nɔrɔ୍kɔ
tumɔrɔ  sɔ୍wɔrij rupre bas kɔre
ebɔŋ tumɔrɔ mukʰre sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ bɔ  sis୍ʈɔ୍jɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ kɔre |

bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maŋ୍kɔ taŋ୍kɔ kɔmɔlɔsiŋhasɔnɔ upre ekaki bɔsitʰile 
sad̤u o sad̤umanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru ebɔŋ sɔrɔ୍pɔ dɔ
 ɖɔ ɔnɔnɔ୍tɔ b̤asuki
hɔ̃ sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi pɔ୍rɔb̤u mũ
tumɔrɔ hɔd͡ʒar hɔd͡ʒar bahu sɔ୍tɔnɔ mukʰ
ebɔŋ akʰi dekʰe  pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek par୍sɔ୍wɔre
pɔrɔpʰek୍ʈɔ bibid̤
ebɔŋ tumɔrɔ kɔ  ɳɔsi sɔ୍tʰan nahĩ keũʈʰi arɔmɔ୍b̤ɔ nahĩ
kɔ  ɳɔsi ken୍dɔ୍rɔ nahĩ sipʰ୍ʈɔsɔ୍ 
d͡ʒeũʈʰare pɔ୍raɳɔrɔ nɔd͡ʒɔrɔ uʈʰe 
tumɔrɔ ken୍dɔ୍rij at୍mɔ sɔrɔ୍bɔbɔ୍japi ebɔŋ sɔrɔ୍bɔbid͡ʒeta
ɔsim rad͡ʒa mũ
tum upre anaɖɔmɔ୍ dekʰut͡ʃʰi
kɔ୍lɔbɔ୍ sel୍ ɖis୍kɔsɔ୍ tumku d͡ʒɔɭutʰiba dekʰ
 ɔsɔhɔ୍jɔ
alୋkɔ pr̩tʰibi sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔ ebɔŋ nɔrɔ୍kɔre
ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒɔ୍jɔୋti alୋkɔ buliba
ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar din pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar
dekʰ mũ d͡ʒek  ɳɔsi upajre
he pɔ୍rɔb̤u mũ tumku upasna kɔre ɔbib̤ad͡ʒit sɔrɔ୍bɔsɔ୍res୍ʈʰɔ
t͡ʃin୍tad̤ara
b̤ɔɳɔ୍ɖarɔpɔ୍rasad
d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ d̤ɔnɔku d̤ɔri rɔkʰiba paĩ kɔla  al pɔ୍rɔdan kɔrad͡ʒait͡ʃʰi |
guɳɔrɔ nijɔmɔku as୍rɔjɔ deba  rɔɳa d͡ʒeũʈʰaru d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ  rɔɳa sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ nɔdir sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒɔɭɔku
ʈaɳitʰae  gɔୋʈie d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mit ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij ɔpɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tit ebɔŋ ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij sɔkɔ୍ti ebɔŋ mɔhima sɔhit ɔtitɔrɔ t͡ʃin୍ta ɔtit dekʰiba




t͡ʃɔnɔ୍dɔ୍rɔrɔ rupa ebɔŋ
sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ suna
tumɔrɔ mɔhan akʰiru gɔ  rɔban୍wit | tumɔrɔ dr̩s୍jɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ kɔୋmɔɭɔ
tara ebɔŋ akasre
us୍mɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔku
tumɔrɔ bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maɳ୍ɖɔku as୍t͡ʃɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔre | dunia as୍t͡ʃɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔre pɔripur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ |
tumɔrɔ sid୍d̤ɔta sɔ୍pes୍
sɔ୍ʈar୍ t͡ʃʰiɲ୍t͡ʃa d͡ʒaitʰiba ebɔŋ sun୍jɔ sɔ୍tʰan
pɔୋlɔru niɭ rɔŋɔ୍gɔrɔ pɔୋlɔ pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ bɔnɔ୍d̤a heba pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek sɔ୍tʰanre
tumku tumku tume  d͡ʒeũʈʰare tume nuhɔ̃
he pɔbit୍rɔ t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar rup keũʈʰare miɭila nahĩ
he rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔmɔjɔ b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ
tumku dekʰi d͡ʒɔɳasuɳa
tʰɔ୍ri war୍lɔ୍ɖɔsɔ୍ b̤ukɔmɔ୍pɔ nim୍nɔ debtamane tumɔrɔ nikɔʈɔtɔrɔ huɔnɔ୍ti
semane semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ papuli guɖ଼ai dele
sɔrir sɔ୍tɔnɔ ebɔŋ bɔ୍rɔୋ
ebɔŋ pʰus୍pʰus୍ upasna tumku pɔ୍rɔsɔnsa o mɔhima kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
 sɔ ebɔŋ sid୍d̤ɔ kan୍dɔnɔ୍ti
nɔmɔsɔ୍kar sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ mɔharad͡ʒ
 si ebɔŋ gajɔkɔŋɔ୍kɔʈʰaru gɔ  rɔbɔrɔ b̤ɔd͡ʒɔnɔ b̤aŋ୍gɔnɔ୍ti ɖɔlɔseʈ୍ sɔ
 har୍dɔ୍dɔ୍jɔre
tumɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔsɔnsa bɔd͡ʒaut͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
ɔgɔɳit kɔmɔ୍pani kahaɳi gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔrutʰibabeɭe
rud୍rɔ d͡ʒie  ɖɔ଼re t͡ʃɔ  nɔ୍ti
tʰɔ adit୍jɔrɔ d͡ʒɔ୍jɔୋtir୍mɔjɔ pʰɔrɔ୍mɔ
b̤as୍ ebɔŋ sad୍̤ja bis୍wɔ usmap
maruʈ୍ ebɔŋ sehi mɔhan d͡ʒaãɭa
sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij nɔ୍jajd͡ʒuk୍tɔ ɔsɔwin୍sɔ
gan୍d̤ɔrɔ୍b̤as୍ rakʰjɔsɔ sid୍d̤ɔ ebɔŋ ɔsura  #  
emane tumku dekʰɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ
hɔʈʰat୍ b̤ɔjɔb̤it b̤ɔjɔre sɔmɔ୍man kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
hɔ̃ dunia  tumku t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar rup sɔhit dekʰiba
t͡ʃehera sɔhit bɔhuguɳit
akʰi sɔhit d͡ʒaha sɔmɔsɔ୍te dekʰɔnɔ୍ti
 ɔsɔŋkʰɔ୍jɔ akʰi bis୍tr̩t bahu sɔdɔsɔ୍jɔmane ɔtuɭnij
sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ ebɔŋ tara sɔhit alୋkit

mũ tumku akasku ag̤at kɔribaku t͡ʃih୍nit kɔre
agre t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar d͡ʒɔ୍ɲani
biraʈ in୍dɔ୍rɔd̤ɔnu t͡ʃit୍rit t͡ʃɔmɔkɔdar ebɔŋ tumɔrɔ paʈi
kʰɔୋlila ebɔŋ ɔrɔ୍bɔsɔ୍ d͡ʒaha
sɔbu dekʰe

he b̤ɔgɔbanɔŋɔ୍kɔ akʰi he he
mɔୋrɔ at୍mar sɔkɔ୍ti pɔɭajɔnɔ hɔୋit͡ʃʰi
t͡ʃalit͡ʃʰi hr̩dɔjɔrɔ sɔkɔ୍ti b̤ɔrɔ୍tɔ୍sɔna heut͡ʃʰi mɔnɔrɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa
d͡ʒetebeɭe mũ tumku dekʰe

sehi ɔgɔ୍ni pɔri b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒaha pr̩tʰibi sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔku gɔ୍ras
kɔrib 
aha mũ mũ pr̩tʰibi ebɔŋ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔ dekʰu nahĩ
he pɔ୍rɔb̤umanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u mũ dekʰut͡ʃʰi
kebɔɭɔ tume
bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mɔୋte dɔja kɔrɔ।
tume duniar sɔrɔɳar୍tʰi
dekʰ
tumɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ gɔɭa ebɔŋ oʈʰ d̤ɔɭa rɔŋɔ୍gɔrɔ gum୍pʰaku mũ
dekʰut͡ʃʰi amɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍b̤ɔ୍ran୍tɔ bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti
mɔhan d̤r̩tras୍ʈɔ୍rɔrɔ put୍rɔ
b̤is୍mɔ ɖɔ୍rɔୋna ebɔŋ kɔrɔ୍na d̤ɔrapɖit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti
kiŋ୍gɔsɔ୍ ebɔŋ mukʰiamane ʈaɳitʰile
sehi pʰaŋ୍ka g̤aʈ
ehi ub̤ɔjɔ sɔ  nɔ୍jɔbahinir sɔrɔ୍bɔୋtɔ୍tɔmɔ t͡ʃʰiɳ୍ɖahୋigla
tum d͡ʒɔhɔ୍nɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre semane
pura rɔkɔ୍tɔre maŋ୍gɔleɖ୍
d̤uɭi ebɔŋ mr̩t୍jure pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti ɖaun୍ɖɔ୍raib୍̤ sɔ୍ʈɔ୍rim୍ pɔri |
ɔsɔhaj tɔtɔ୍pɔrɔta sɔhit d͡ʒaha
kɔ୍rɔୋd̤it pɔ୍rɔbahre
sid̤a sɔɭɔkʰɔ sɔmud୍rɔrɔ gɔlɔ୍pʰiŋ୍gɔ୍ gɔb̤irku d͡ʒae
teɳu sehi d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ୍tɔ gum୍pʰaku
sehi birmane mɔhan ebɔŋ sahsi  aɭ ɔnɔnɔ୍tɔ
sɔ୍rɔୋtɔre ɔsɔhaj gɔti sɔhit
pɔୋkɔ pɔri d͡ʒaha ratire
ek alୋkɔ aɖku 
ulutʰae semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ୍tɔ bipɔdɔku ʈaɳi uɖ଼iba ebɔŋ mɔriba
teɳu semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mr̩t୍ju pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ b̤iɖ଼
ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔ t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kr̩t nirɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ b̤abre bɔhɔnɔ
kɔre sehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒɔnɔta bɔɳua uɖ଼aɳ
tum୍eb̤ esmaen purusmanɔŋɔ୍ku
pɔrit୍d͡ʒag kɔriɔt͡ʃʰɔ

d͡ʒeũ pɔ୍raɳimanɔŋɔ୍ku tume
tiari kɔrɔ d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒɔhɔ୍nɔ sɔhit tume gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔrɔ semanɔŋɔ୍ku lap୍
kɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u b̤ɔgɔban tumɔrɔ atɔŋɔ୍kɔ
pr̩tʰibir sesru ses pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ
d͡ʒibɔnɔ pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔru
mr̩t୍ju pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ marat୍mɔkɔ d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔnɔ୍tɔ lɔୋriɖ୍ b̤ɔjɔ sɔhit
aha bis୍ɳu mɔୋte d͡ʒɔɳan୍tu

nɔmɔୋsɔ୍ʈu ʈi debb̤araŋ୍ku pɔ୍rɔɳam kɔre pɔ୍rɔsad  # 
he mɔhan୍ pɔ୍rɔb̤u rihɔrɔ୍sal୍
kahĩki tume ete b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ sam୍na kɔrut͡ʃʰ
ehi digʈi b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ ɔgɔ୍rɔgɔti keũʈʰaru t͡ʃalib
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
tume mɔୋte sɔmɔjɔ b̤ɔɭi dekʰut͡ʃʰ d͡ʒie hɔtɔ୍ja kɔre
sɔmɔjɔ d͡ʒie sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku binas kɔre
hɔtɔ୍jakari sɔmɔjɔ pɔ୍rat͡ʃin din gɔ୍ras kɔribaku eʈʰaku as
tum bɔ୍jɔtit ehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sɔtɔ୍ru mukʰia sɔd͡ʒɔ୍d͡ʒit
d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔkʰjet୍rɔku kehi d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ t͡ʃʰaɖibe nahĩ niras
au nahĩ uʈʰ pɔ୍rɔsid୍d̤ɔ pɔ୍rap୍tɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍tu tum୍b̤ɔrɔ sɔtɔ୍rumanɔŋɔ୍ku binas kɔrɔ।
d͡ʒetebeɭe tume seguɖ଼iku pɔras୍tɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰ sehi rad͡ʒ୍jɔ paĩ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ kɔrɔ |
mɔୋ dɔ୍wara semane pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti  tume nuhẽ mr̩t୍jur ag̤at semanɔŋɔ୍ku bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mukabila kɔrad͡ʒait͡ʃʰi
d͡ʒepri semane ehipri b̤abre t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar b̤abre pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti tume mɔୋrɔ bad୍jɔd͡ʒɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ
sɔ୍ʈɔ୍raik୍ sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi sɔsɔsɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ pɔ୍rin୍sɔ ɖɔ୍rɔୋnare b̤is୍mɔ d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔg̤ɔʈɔre mr̩t୍ju karbar
kɔrɔna d͡ʒɔjɔdɔ୍ratʰa semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ pɔri nis୍wasre ruh
mũ semanɔŋɔ୍ku binɔsɔ୍ʈɔ kɔre tume hɔtɔ୍ja kɔrib kin୍tu hɔtɔ୍ja kɔrib
d͡ʒud୍d̤ɔ semane nis୍t͡ʃɔjɔ pɔɖɔ଼ibe ebɔŋ tume nis୍t͡ʃɔjɔ bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃib ehi sɔmɔtɔɭɔ b̤umire bid͡ʒji
sɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔjɔ |
sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi kesɔbɔŋɔ୍kɔ bak୍jɔ suɳi
kɔmɔ୍pit hɔୋi pɔ୍rɔb̤uŋ୍ku sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ
kɔritʰiba taŋ୍kɔ papuli bɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔri ebɔŋ 
kr̩s୍ɳɔŋɔ୍kɔ ɔnug୍rɔhɔ pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kɔri seʈʰare ʈʰia hɔୋi kɔhile
nɔtɔmɔsɔ୍tɔkɔ ebɔŋ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃarɔɳɔ b̤aŋ୍gi
ehi sɔbɔ୍dɔguɖ଼ik sɔmɔjanusare kɔtʰit
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
mul୍jɔban pɔ୍rɔb̤u pɔ୍rɔb̤u
sɔmɔgɔ୍rɔ bis୍wɔ
tum୍b̤ɔrɔ ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik sɔkɔ୍tire anɔnɔ୍dit hue। rakʰjɔsɔ tumku dekʰi
b̤ɔjɔb̤it hɔୋi t͡ʃari t͡ʃɔtur୍tʰansɔku dɔ୍rut gɔtire gɔle ebɔŋ kɔmɔ୍pani


sid୍d̤ɔŋɔ୍kɔ nam tumɔrɔ nam |
semane kipri
tumɔrɔ mɔhima  sɔ୍wɔrij sɔkɔ୍tisaɭi g̤ɔୋsɔɳa kɔribe nahĩ
tume bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍ma bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍maʈʰaru bɔɖɔ଼
tume ɔsim sr̩s୍ʈikɔrɔ୍tɔ୍ta
he debtamanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ b̤ɔgɔban d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ basɔsɔ୍tʰan ebɔŋ bis୍ram
tume sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ pɔ୍raɳru
bu  iba pura
gɔʈʰɔnɔ heba ebɔŋ pʰɔ୍remɔrɔ୍ heba b̤ɔɭi ruphin

bɔɖɔʈʰaru bɔɖɔ d͡ʒie
d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ d̤ɔnɔ sɔhit d͡ʒɔgɔtɔku gɔt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃʰit kɔla he b̤ɔɳɔ୍ɖardabidar
kie sɔbuʈʰu b̤ɔlɔ ebɔŋ
nid͡ʒe d͡ʒɔ୍ɲan he b̤ag

 rɔ tɔrɔŋɔ୍gɔ heut͡ʃʰi tumɔrɔ tɔrɔŋɔ୍gɔ | t͡ʃɔnɔ୍dɔ୍rɔ ebɔŋ tara alୋkɔ
tumɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔd͡ʒapti
tume ebɔŋ tumku
eha puratɔnɔ d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ dur alୋkɔku pud͡ʒa kɔribare aɳ୍ʈʰumaɖi
mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔ purusmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru pɔ୍rɔtʰɔmɔ |
punɔrɔ୍bar he b̤ɔgɔban punɔrɔ୍bar
ek hɔd͡ʒar hɔd͡ʒar tʰɔrɔ br̩d୍d̤i kɔrɔ

ebɔŋ pɔ୍rɔsɔnsa  tum

eʈʰare upre tɔɭe
kan୍dila d͡ʒetebeɭe tume d͡ʒib

namୋsɔ୍ʈu b̤ɔgɔban upasna kɔle
namୋsɔ୍ʈu namhin pɔ୍rɔb̤u

a  d͡ʒɔdi bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔre
tume mɔne rɔkʰiba ut͡ʃit୍ mũ b̤abili tum bɔnɔ୍d̤u

d͡ʒat୍ra sɔmɔjɔre kim୍ba tʰɔʈɔ୍ʈare
kim୍ba d͡ʒetebeɭe ame bis୍ram neba
pɔrisɔdɔre bɔsi gɔ୍rib̤re b̤ɔ୍rɔmɔɳɔ kɔriba
ekaki kim୍ba b̤iɖ଼re tumku

upɔrɔୋkɔ୍tɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ pita |
gurumanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ guru d͡ʒahaki adɔrɔkari ebɔŋ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔʈʰaru ɔd̤ik

kr̩s୍ɳɔ
hɔ̃ tume dekʰit͡ʃʰ ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun karɔɳɔ mũ tumku b̤ɔlɔ pautʰili
mɔୋrɔ gup୍tɔ mukʰ rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔmɔjɔ mɔnɔ୍tɔ୍rɔ
d͡ʒɔ୍jɔୋti ebɔŋ t͡ʃɔmɔtɔ୍kar ebɔŋ bis୍tr̩t mɔhima bɔhuguɳ dɔ୍wara pɔ୍rɔkasit
d͡ʒaha tumku bɔrɔ୍sɔsara bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃaibaku kehi pɔsɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔrintʰile
karɔɳɔ bed
dɔ୍  ara eha ase nahĩ kim୍ba bɔɭidan kim୍ba b̤ikʰja kim୍ba b̤ɔlɔ kam kɔre nahĩ kim୍ba dir୍g̤ɔ sɔmɔjɔ ɔnutap kɔre nahĩ kim୍ba pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kɔre nahĩ kim୍ba
git gan kɔre nahĩ
sehi mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔrɔ akʰi ɔmɔrɔ at୍maku dekʰiba paĩ  kurusɔrɔ
rad͡ʒkumar eha kebɔɭɔ tum paĩ rɔkʰad͡ʒaitʰila kʰusi huɔ
au tumɔrɔ hr̩dɔjɔku hɔlaibaku diɔ nahĩ karɔɳɔ tumɔrɔ akʰi
mɔୋrɔ gɔ  rɔbɔ sɔhit mɔୋrɔ atɔŋɔ୍kɔ dekʰit͡ʃʰi | mũ d͡ʒepri pur୍bɔpɔri tʰili
mũ punɔrɔ୍bar tum paĩ rɔhibi haluka hr̩dɔjɔ sɔhit dekʰ

bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mũ dekʰut͡ʃʰi d͡ʒanar୍ɖana
ehi bɔnɔ୍d̤ut୍wɔpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ manɔbɔ pʰɔ୍rem୍ mɔୋ mɔnɔ
puɳi tʰɔre san୍tɔ t͡ʃin୍ta kɔriparib mɔୋrɔ hr̩dɔjɔ puɳi tʰɔre ag̤at kɔre
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
hɔ̃
pɔ୍rij rad͡ʒkumar tume d͡ʒepri dekʰil taha dekʰiba ɔtɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ as୍t͡ʃɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔd͡ʒɔnɔkɔ ebɔŋ b̤ɔjɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ tʰila  debtamane
b̤ɔjɔb̤it ebɔŋ nirɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ dekʰiba paĩ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
tɔtʰapi bed dɔ୍wara nuhẽ bɔɭidanru
na ɔnutap na uphar deba kim୍ba pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna sɔhit nuhẽ
 d͡ʒepri tume dekʰit͡ʃʰ
kebɔɭɔ pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ seba sid୍d̤ɔ bis୍ 
as ebɔŋ ɔtɔ୍jɔd̤ik at୍mɔsɔmɔrɔ୍pɔɳɔ dɔ୍wara mũ d͡ʒɔɳasuɳa
ebɔŋ b̤artij pɔ୍rin୍sɔku dekʰili ebɔŋ pɔ୍rɔbes kɔli
d͡ʒie mɔୋ paĩ sɔbu kɔrɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒie mɔୋte kʰɔୋd͡ʒɔnɔ୍ti
 sɔrɔ୍bɔda adɔrɔ kɔre
mũ d͡ʒaha tiari kɔrit͡ʃʰi ebɔŋ mũ pɔ୍rem kɔre pɔ୍remɔrɔ ekmat୍rɔ ses paĩ sehi
bɔ୍jɔkɔ୍ti ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun mɔୋ pakʰku d͡ʒaut͡ʃʰi।
eʈʰare ekadɔsɔ ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ses | b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍ gita

ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj
ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
pɔ୍rɔb̤u d͡ʒeũmane tumku seba kɔrɔnɔ୍ti semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru  hr̩dɔjɔre sɔtɔ୍jɔ 
d͡ʒepri  sɔ୍bɔrɔ pɔ୍rɔkas kɔrit͡ʃʰɔnɔ୍ti ebɔŋ seba kɔrutʰiba purusmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru
 tumku upasna kɔri pɔ୍rɔkasit ɔbib̤ɔkɔ୍tɔ dur keũmane
bis୍was ebɔŋ d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ ut୍tɔmɔ mar୍gɔ niɔnɔ୍ti
kr̩s୍ɳɔ
d͡ʒie mɔୋrɔ seba kɔre  d͡ʒepri mũ nid͡ʒku dekʰae 
nirɔnɔ୍tɔrɔ sɔtɔ୍jɔ pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ b̤ɔkɔ୍tire sɔ୍tʰir
d͡ʒeũmane mɔୋte bɔhut pɔbit୍rɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti | kin୍tu kie seba kɔre 
mɔୋte upasna kɔrutʰiba d͡ʒɔɳe ɔdr̩s୍jɔ
pɔ୍rɔkasit namhin
ɔbaɲ୍t͡ʃʰit sɔrɔ୍bɔsɔ୍res୍ʈʰɔ sɔrɔ୍bɔbɔ୍japi sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ nis୍t͡ʃit 
d͡ʒie mɔୋte ehipri adɔrɔ kɔre semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ b̤abnaku ajɔtɔ୍tɔ kɔre
sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ ek sɔ୍tʰir mɔnɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍te kʰusi | b̤ɔlɔ

  mɔୋ sɔhit ek at୍ma ​​|
d͡ʒie ehipri nid͡ʒku d͡ʒaɳe ebɔŋ taŋ୍kɔ at୍ma ​​pursaku d͡ʒaɳe pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir mɔୋɖɔ୍ sɔhit
guɳguɖik mad୍̤jɔmɔre kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ kɔre alୋkɔ taŋ୍kɔ paĩ asit͡ʃʰi se d͡ʒaha bi mansɔ bɔhɔnɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti se au kebe b̤ar bɔhɔnɔ kɔribe nahĩ | seʈʰare kit͡ʃʰi ɔɭɔ୍pɔ lɔୋkɔ d̤ɔ୍jan dɔ୍wara at୍mɔbid୍jaɭɔjɔre pɔ୍raɳ kʰɔୋd͡ʒɔnɔ୍ti au ketek lɔmɔ୍ba dɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ dɔ୍wara ebɔŋ pɔbit୍rɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ seʈʰare pɔhɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃe ketek kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ dɔ୍wara ketek kɔdapi ete pɔ୍rap୍tɔ hue nahĩ alୋkɔrɔ sɔbɔ୍dɔ ɔnɔ୍jɔ oʈʰru suɳ ebɔŋ ehaku d̤ɔri rɔkʰɔ ebɔŋ upasna kɔrɔ hɔ̃ ebɔŋ seguɖ଼ik  sɔtɔ୍jɔ sikʰja deba  mr̩t୍juku ɔtik୍rɔmɔ kɔrɔ










d͡ʒeũʈʰare bi b̤artij pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
d͡ʒibɔnɔ heut͡ʃʰi  gɔtisiɭ d͡ʒinis kim୍ba d͡ʒinisguɖik sɔ୍tʰanan୍tɔrit
ud୍b̤id kim୍ba tɔtʰapi bihɔnɔ  d͡ʒaɳ
bɔsɔ୍tu ebɔŋ at୍ma ​​bɔnɔ୍d̤ɔnɔre kɔɳɔ bɔ  it͡ʃʰi d͡ʒaɳ
d͡ʒe se pɔ୍rɔkr̩tre dekʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒie
d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ pɔ୍rɔb̤u pɔ୍raɳku sɔman b̤abre dekʰɔnɔ୍ti | binas mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre at୍ma ​​sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ
ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij
karɔɳɔ d͡ʒie ehipri dekʰe pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek sɔ୍tʰanre
pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek rupre sɔman gɔୋʈie d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ ​​nid͡ʒ paĩ
au kɔ  ɳɔsi ɔnɔ୍jaj kɔre nahĩ
kin୍tu sɔrɔ୍bɔୋt͡ʃɔ୍t͡ʃɔ ras୍ta d͡ʒae d͡ʒaha sukʰ aɳitʰae |
dekʰi se dekʰɔnɔ୍ti pɔ୍rɔkr̩tre d͡ʒie dekʰɔnɔ୍ti d͡ʒe
pɔ୍rɔkr̩tir ɔb̤ɔ୍jas pɔ୍raɳ
ɔb̤inɔjɔ dɔ୍wara ɔb̤ɔ୍jas kɔriba paĩ tɔtʰapi ed͡ʒeɳ୍ʈɔ nuhẽ
ɔlɔga d͡ʒibɔd͡ʒɔnɔ୍tuŋ୍kɔ b̤iɖ଼ dekʰe  ehar pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek pɔ୍rɔkar 
gɔୋʈieru is୍ju ebɔŋ punɔrɔ୍bar gɔୋʈie sɔhit mis୍rɔɳɔ kɔrɔ
tapre se bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍ma ɔt͡ʃʰi se pɔ୍rap୍tɔ kɔre
he rad͡ʒkumar
sehi t͡ʃɔrɔmɔ ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ at୍ma sr̩s୍ʈi
ɔd͡ʒɔୋgɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒetebeɭe eha sɔrirre pɔ୍rɔbes kɔre
kɔ  ɳɔsi kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔrɔ dag nɔtʰae kit͡ʃʰi kam kɔre nahĩ
itʰeral୍ baju pɔri sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku bɔ୍japitʰae
d͡ʒaha ɔti sukʰj୍mɔta paĩ kɔɭɔŋɔ୍kɔru durei d͡ʒae
sukʰj୍mɔ pɔ୍raɳ sɔbu sɔ୍tʰanre bɔsitʰae ɔpɔris୍kar
sɔrɔ୍bɔpɔ୍rɔtʰɔmɔ sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔŋɔ୍kɔ alୋkɔ pɔri
d͡ʒaha alୋkit heba dɔ୍wara pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tit hue nahĩ
pɔ୍raɳɔrɔ | pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek sɔ୍tʰanre alୋkɔ sud୍d̤ɔ hue
ebɔŋ d͡ʒeũmane d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanɔrɔ akʰire dekʰɔnɔ୍ti
kete gurut୍wɔpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ ebɔŋ eha sɔhit kɔɳɔ karbar hue semane b̤ag kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
ebɔŋ at୍ma ​​ebɔŋ sɔrir kipri  gɔɖa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
sehi d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanimane d͡ʒibɔnɔku nei d͡ʒaan୍ti
eʈʰare ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ɔd̤ɔ୍jaj ses hue | b̤ɔgɔbɔdɔ୍ gita
akʰ୍ja bisis୍ʈɔ kʰjet୍rekʰjet୍rɔd͡ʒɔnab̤ib̤gajୋgɔ୍
kim୍ba bɔsɔ୍tu ebɔŋ at୍ma ​​pr̩tʰɔkɔ b̤abre d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ pus୍tɔkɔ।

sɔhɔb̤agitaku bɔ  ଼nɔ୍ti

 kim୍ba pɔ୍rɔlijɔsɔre pɔribɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔnɔ hue nahĩ

mata pɔ୍rɔtɔ୍jek mɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔ୍jɔ rup bɔ୍rɔhɔ୍ma gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔd̤arɔɳɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti

ebɔŋ alୋkit d͡ʒibɔnɔd͡ʒapɔnɔ
paphin at୍maku sukʰ ebɔŋ sɔtɔ୍jɔre ban୍d̤idie

mansɔ paĩ sukʰɔdɔ d͡ʒɔ୍ɲanre ebɔŋ pas୍ ban୍d̤e |

sehi sɔhɔrɔre sɔ୍tʰir hɔୋitʰiba sutʰpʰas୍ʈen୍sɔ rad͡ʒɔtɔ୍wɔ kɔripare |

ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar ebɔŋ ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar ɔɭɔsua ebɔŋ ɔsɔ୍tʰirta ɔt͡ʃʰi

hue eha sehi sɔ୍tʰanku d͡ʒae
 d͡ʒeũmane sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ sɔtɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔru sid୍d̤ɔ ebɔŋ nir୍mɔɭɔ |

sɔbud͡ʒ ebɔŋ tɔrɔŋɔ୍gɔ b̤ɔd͡ʒɔnɔ d͡ʒaha sɔtɔ୍jɔku pʰus୍pʰus୍ kɔre
kie aswatʰa d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti bed ebɔŋ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔŋɔ୍ku d͡ʒaɳɔnɔ୍ti |
ehar sakʰa sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔku guɭi kɔri pr̩tʰibiku buɖ଼id͡ʒae  # 
mɔnus୍jɔrɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ d͡ʒepri semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔre
guɳru ehar rupa sɔ୍pɔ୍re ebɔŋ pʰul
ebɔŋ ehar gɔrɔ୍bɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ut୍sah
t͡ʃum୍bɔnɔre sig୍̤rɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔku lɔmɔ୍pʰɔ diɔ | sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ ebɔŋ pɔbɔnɔrɔ
d͡ʒehetu purusmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ pɔ୍rɔlɔୋb̤ɔnɔ meɭaku tɔ୍wɔran୍wit kɔre
 ehar  ulutʰiba muɭguɖ଼ik
tɔɭe tʰiba maʈi kʰɔୋd͡ʒe ehaku d̤ɔri rɔkʰibare sahad͡ʒ୍jɔ kɔre
mɔnus୍jɔrɔ ehi dunia mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔkɔɭap d͡ʒepri
punɔrɔ୍bar bɔnɔ୍d̤ɔnɔ dɔ୍wara semanɔŋɔ୍ku ban୍d̤ɔ |
d͡ʒɔdi tume gɔt͡ʃʰɔrɔ sikʰjaku b̤ɔlɔ b̤abre d͡ʒaɳitʰil
ehar akr̩ti kɔɳɔ kɔhitʰae ebɔŋ eha keũʈʰaru ut୍pɔnɔ୍nɔ hue au ta pɔre
eha kipri sɔmap୍tɔ heb ebɔŋ ehar sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ ɔsubid̤a
tikʰj୍ɳɔ bit͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰin୍nɔtar kura  ଼i apɔɳɔ t͡ʃahĩbe
ebɔŋ aliŋ୍gɔnɔ kɔrutʰiba sapɔrɔ muɭku kʰɔɳɔ୍ɖɔ kʰɔɳɔ୍ɖɔ kɔridebe ebɔŋ
ehi aswatʰaku nim୍nɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ d̤arɔɳɔ kɔribe  seʈ୍ kɔribaku |
sehi sukʰi akasre nutɔnɔ ɔb̤ibr̩d୍d̤i 
d͡ʒeũmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ pakʰre pɔhɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃe semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ mɔribar din rɔhib nahĩ
kim୍ba lɔୋpɔ paib nahĩ kim୍ba pɔɖɔ଼ib nahĩ  taŋ୍kɔ paĩ mɔୋrɔ ɔrɔ୍tʰɔ
pita ebɔŋ pɔ୍rɔtʰɔmɔ d͡ʒie rɔhɔsɔ୍jɔ sr̩s୍ʈi kɔritʰile |
puratɔnɔ sr̩s୍ʈir karɔɳɔ semane
ut୍sahru ebɔŋ sɔ୍wɔpɔ୍nɔru durei d͡ʒaan୍ti
kie semanɔŋɔ୍ku bɔnɔ୍d̤ɔnɔre ban୍d̤i rɔkʰe
ebɔŋ  sɔrɔ୍bɔୋpɔri se sɔrɔ୍bɔda upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍ti 

gɔ୍ris୍mɔ b̤ɔୋgɔrɔ pɔbɔnɔ sɔୋitʰiba gɔt͡ʃʰɔku
dɔୋhɔlai die nahĩ pɔ୍rɔbɔɭɔ  ɖɔ଼rɔ bis୍pʰɔୋrɔɳɔ semanɔŋɔ୍ku t͡ʃiridie ɖaɭ ebɔŋ sɔ୍ʈem୍
ɔnɔnɔ୍tɔ duniaku eb̤ɭi pas୍ kɔre
seʈʰare au ek sur୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ ud͡ʒ୍d͡ʒɔ୍wɔɭɔ ɔnɔ୍jɔ ek t͡ʃɔnɔ୍dɔ୍rɔ

ɔbis୍mɔrɔɳij at୍ma

sen୍sɔ ebɔŋ bud୍d̤i | sar୍bɔb̤ɔ  mɔ pɔ୍raɳ

ebɔŋ sɔmanta ebɔŋ dan

tr̩p୍tɔ hr̩dɔjɔ d̤ɔ  rɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ dr̩  ta ebɔŋ sud୍d̤ɔta
sɔhit purusୋtɔ୍tɔmɔ sɔhit mis୍rit b̤ɔdɔ୍rɔ nɔmɔ୍rɔ ebɔŋ kɔbɔrɔ ek pɔ୍rɔtisୋd̤ɔpɔrajɔɳɔ at୍ma nid͡ʒku ɔd̤ik ut͡ʃ୍t͡ʃɔ kɔribaku kebe diad͡ʒai nahĩ  ehipri t͡ʃih୍nɔguɖik



he b̤artij rad͡ʒkumar d͡ʒahar pad sɔ୍tʰapit hɔୋit͡ʃʰi

pɔ୍rɔtarɳa ɔhɔŋkar ebɔŋ ɔhɔŋkar

ebɔŋ ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲɔta nid͡ʒ ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkarku ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔ 
eguɖ଼ik heut͡ʃʰi t͡ʃih୍nɔ mɔୋrɔ rad͡ʒkumar d͡ʒahar d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ
mɔnɔ୍dɔ ɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃɔɭɔ paĩ b̤ag୍jɔban |  # 
sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ muk୍ti aɳe
teɳu tume d͡ʒaɳiba ut͡ʃit୍ ɔsuras sɔhit d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ
bɔnɔ୍d̤ɔnɔre pɔriɳɔtɔ hue | he anɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔrɔ rad͡ʒkumar
d͡ʒahar lɔʈɔ sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ paĩ pr̩tʰɔkɔ hɔୋit͡ʃʰi |
seʈʰare duiʈi sɔ୍ʈam୍pɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ d͡ʒibɔnɔ୍tɔ purus
ɖib̤ain୍ ebɔŋ ɔɳɔ୍ɖaib̤ain୍ upre t͡ʃih୍nit hɔୋit͡ʃʰi mũ tumku kɔhili
tume keũ t͡ʃih୍nɔ dɔ୍wara sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gij mɔɳisku d͡ʒaɳiba ut͡ʃit୍

at୍mamane mɔୋʈʰaru kipri baharku d͡ʒaan୍ti kim୍ba semane kipri
mɔୋ pakʰku pʰeri asɔnɔ୍ti kim୍ba setʰire sɔtɔ୍jɔta nahĩ
kim୍ba sud୍d̤ɔta kim୍ba d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ nijɔmɔ nahĩ | teɳu semane kuhɔnɔ୍ti ehi d͡ʒɔgɔtɔrɔ
kɔ  ɳɔsi nijɔmɔ nahĩ ki ades na pɔ୍rɔb̤u teɳu semane kuhɔnɔ୍ti kim୍ba karɔɳɔ ɔnusɔrɔɳɔ kɔri
uʈʰi nahãnɔ୍ti  sɔmpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ ud୍des୍jɔre kin୍tu ɔnɔ୍jɔ kehi nuhɔ̃nɔ୍ti। ebɔŋ ehi d͡ʒinis t͡ʃin୍ta kɔrut͡ʃʰi sehi sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ nɔsɔ୍ʈɔ hɔୋid͡ʒaitʰiba  ɔɭɔ୍pɔ t͡ʃɔtur ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkarɔmɔjɔ  nid͡ʒku mɔnɔ୍dɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ nid͡ʒku ɔb̤isap diɔ | ɔsɔnɔ୍tus୍ʈɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰare at୍mɔsɔmɔrɔ୍pɔɳɔ pɔ୍rɔtarɳa mur୍kʰɔta ebɔŋ gɔrɔ୍bɔre pɔripur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔtare semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ tɔ୍ruʈire ban୍d̤i pappur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ pɔtʰɔre d̤ɔrapɖigɔla semane ehi mitʰ୍ja upre bis୍was kɔrɔnɔ୍ti |









d͡ʒehetu eha sɔtɔ୍jɔ tʰila  ehi mitʰ୍ja d͡ʒaha mr̩t୍juku neitʰae

nis୍kɔ୍rij b̤ɔrɔsa mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre
dasmane semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ abeg ebɔŋ kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔrɔ das semane
muɭ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ sɔhit d̤ɔnɔ kɔ୍rɔjɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti gɔrɔmɔ b̤ɔୋkɔku b̤ɔriba paĩ
semane kɔhɔnɔ୍ti ad͡ʒi pɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ am୍b̤emane hasɔlɔ kɔrit͡ʃʰu
ehipri hr̩dɔjɔrɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ heb
ebɔŋ eha amɔrɔ ebɔŋ ɔnɔ୍jɔ amɔrɔ heb
ad͡ʒi ame ek sɔtɔ୍ruku hɔtɔ୍ja kɔlu ebɔŋ asɔnɔ୍takali ame amɔrɔ ɔnɔ୍jɔ sɔtɔ୍ruku hɔtɔ୍ja

amɔrɔ b̤ag୍jɔ pɔ୍rɔsid୍d̤ɔ sahsi ebɔŋ mɔhan nuhẽ ki
ame d̤ɔni gɔrɔ୍bɔrɔ sɔhit d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ ɔnɔ୍jɔ purusmane
am paĩ kipri bas kɔrɔnɔ୍ti hɔtɔ୍ja  tapre bɔɭidan paĩ
bɔɖɔ଼ akarre kas୍ʈɔ kɔrɔ ebɔŋ anɔnɔ୍dɔ kɔrɔ  teɳu semane
ɔd͡ʒɔ୍ɲɔta dɔ୍wara ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkarre kɔtʰa huɔnɔ୍ti teɳu semane pɔɖɔ଼nɔ୍ti 
pɔ୍rɔୋd͡ʒek୍ʈɔ sɔhit ʈɔsɔ୍ ʈɔsɔ୍ pɔ୍rɔtarit ebɔŋ bɔnɔ୍d̤a
kɔɭa b̤ɔ୍ran୍tir d͡ʒalre lɔୋb̤ɔre hɔd͡ʒigla  narakaku
kʰɔrap kɔribaku | d̤ar୍mik pɔ୍rij
d͡ʒid୍kʰɔୋrɔ ebɔŋ gɔrɔ୍bi d̤anɔrɔ mɔdɔ sɔhit mɔdɔ୍jɔpɔ
 ebɔŋ beprua semanɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ sɔmɔsɔ୍tɔ nɔ  bed୍jɔ
kebɔɭɔ sɔmɔ୍manɔrɔ ek pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ
pɔ୍rat͡ʃin bis୍wasɔrɔ d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔre tiari kɔrad͡ʒai nahĩ | ehipri b̤abre
at୍mɔhuɖ୍ bɔɭɔ ɔsɔmɔ୍man b̤ɔୋd͡ʒi kɔ୍rɔୋd̤ɔ
ehi mɔୋrɔ nin୍dakarimane semane pin୍d̤utʰiba rupre
ebɔŋ semane d͡ʒeũ pɔ୍rɔd͡ʒɔnɔnɔ kɔrɔnɔ୍ti mɔୋrɔ sɔtɔ୍rumane
g̤r̩ɳakari ebɔŋ g̤r̩ɳa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti nis୍ʈʰur mɔnɔ୍dɔ mɔnɔ୍dɔ
sɔrɔ୍bɔnim୍nɔ ebɔŋ sɔrɔ୍bɔnim୍nɔ purus d͡ʒahaŋ୍ku mũ
punɔrɔ୍bar pɔkai deitʰili ebɔŋ punɔrɔ୍bar d͡ʒibɔnɔrɔ sesre
kit͡ʃʰi sɔjɔtanɔrɔ gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔre keũʈʰaru  d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔru d͡ʒɔnɔ୍mɔ 
sɔjɔtanɔrɔ gɔrɔ୍b̤ɔguɖ଼ik semanɔŋɔ୍ku punɔrɔ୍bar pɔ୍rɔsɔbɔ kɔle sɔmɔsɔ୍te pɔ୍rɔtarɳa kɔle | 
ebɔŋ d͡ʒepɔrɔ୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔnɔ୍tɔ semane mɔୋte kʰɔୋd͡ʒi pud͡ʒa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti miʈʰa pɔ୍rin୍sɔ
sehi nedɔrɔ rɔୋɖɔku semane pad diɔnɔ୍tu |

ɔrɔ୍d͡ʒun।
d͡ʒɔdi lɔୋkɔmane pɔbit୍rɔ nijɔmɔ pɔrit୍jag kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
sas୍tɔ୍riŋ୍kɔ pɔ୍rɔti ɔbɔheɭa kɔrɔnɔ୍ti tɔtʰapi hr̩dɔjɔre bis୍was rɔkʰɔnɔ୍tu
ebɔŋ upasna kɔrɔnɔ୍tu
mɔhan kr̩s୍ɳɔŋɔ୍kɔrɔ ɔbɔsɔ୍tʰa kɔɳɔ heb sɔtɔ୍jɔwan୍ rad͡ʒɔsɔ୍ tɔmas୍ kuh
kr̩s୍ɳɔ

d͡ʒepriki sɔ୍rikʰjet୍rɔ

b̤uʈasɔŋɔ୍ku pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna
kɔrɔnɔ୍ti
। abegbeseʈ hinsat୍mɔkɔ d͡ʒɔŋɔ୍gɔli nir୍d͡ʒatna  nir୍bɔୋd̤ɔmane  mɔୋrɔ upadanguɖ଼ik semanɔŋɔ୍kɔ mansɔ mɔd̤ɔ୍jɔre nɔ୍jajpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ kɔmɔ୍panire bɔnɔ୍dɔ




na mũ nid͡ʒe mansɔ b̤itre upɔsɔ୍tʰit
semanɔŋɔ୍ku sɔ୍wɔrɔ୍gɔku nuhẽ ut୍sɔrɔ୍gikr̩t b̤utmanɔŋɔ୍kɔ paĩ d͡ʒaɳ
d͡ʒepri kʰad୍jɔ manɔbɔd͡ʒati paĩ tiniguɳ
pus୍ʈikɔrɔ sehipri
upasna nibr̩t୍tɔta ebɔŋ kʰjɔma pɔ୍rar୍tʰɔna kɔribar tiniguɳ upaj ɔt͡ʃʰi
mɔୋrɔ eha suɳ seʈʰare ek kʰad୍jɔ ɔt͡ʃʰi d͡ʒaha
bɔɭɔ pɔdar୍tʰɔ sɔkɔ୍ti ebɔŋ sɔ୍was୍tʰɔ୍jɔ ebɔŋ anɔnɔ୍dɔku bɔɲɔ୍t͡ʃiba paĩ aɳitʰae

 ebɔŋ d͡ʒɔɭutʰiba rɔkɔ୍tɔ ebɔŋ du  kʰɔ

kep୍ʈɔ lab̤ hebar kɔ  ɳɔsi asa bina hr̩dɔjɔ dɔ୍wara ut୍sɔrɔ୍gikr̩t
sɔtɔ୍jɔwanɔrɔ sɔmɔ୍pur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ kar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ pɔ୍rɔkr̩t bis୍was |
gɔrɔ୍bɔ pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔ pɔ୍rɔdɔrɔ୍sɔnɔre dekʰad͡ʒaitʰiba d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ
b̤ɔlɔ mɔnɔୋrɔɲɔ୍d͡ʒɔnɔ upasna kʰɔ୍jati d͡ʒitiba paĩ
d͡ʒepri  mũ kɔhibi  rad͡ʒɔsɔ୍ rasi ebɔŋ br̩tʰa |
d̤ɔrɔ୍mɔ ek nir୍bɔୋd̤ɔ it͡ʃ୍t͡ʃʰa dɔ୍  ara
at୍mɔku nir୍d͡ʒatna deba kim୍ba ɔnɔ୍jɔku ag̤at kɔriba paĩ kʰjɔmɔtaku asiba
  tɔmasɔrɔ ɔnɔ୍d̤ɔkar ebɔŋ ɔsus୍tʰɔta |
upharɔʈi sɔ୍nehpur୍ɳɔ୍ɳɔ b̤abre diagla d͡ʒetebeɭe d͡ʒɔɳe kɔhib
bɔrɔ୍tɔ୍tɔman mũ kʰusire debi d͡ʒetebeɭe se nie se
kit͡ʃʰi pʰerai parib nahĩ nir୍dɔ୍dis୍ʈɔ sɔ୍tʰanre nir୍mit d̤ar୍d͡ʒɔ୍jɔ
sɔmɔjɔ ebɔŋ ek sakʰjat pɔ୍rap୍tɔkɔrɔ୍tɔ୍taŋ୍ku
sɔtɔwanɔrɔ uphar nɔ୍jajd͡ʒuk୍tɔ ebɔŋ lab̤dajɔkɔ ɔʈe |
uphar sɔ୍  ar୍tʰɔpɔrɔ b̤abre diagla keũʈʰare gɔ୍rɔhɔɳɔ kɔrad͡ʒib
punɔrɔ୍bar asa kɔrad͡ʒae kim୍ba d͡ʒetebeɭe kit͡ʃʰi ses kʰɔୋd͡ʒad͡ʒae
kim୍ba d͡ʒeũʈʰare upharɔʈi kɔ୍rɔୋd̤it hue
eha rad͡ʒar ɔʈe im୍pul୍ ɔsus୍tʰɔ |
upharɔʈi kʰɔrap sɔmɔjɔre kʰɔrap sɔmɔjɔre
b̤ul୍ sɔ୍tʰanre ad̤ar pɔ୍rap୍tɔkɔrɔ୍tɔ୍taŋ୍ku
ɔbɔmanna kim୍ba kɔʈʰɔୋrɔ ɔparɔgɔta tamasɔrɔ
